Asmekti n tefsut n 80 akked tefsut taberkant
Tacemmaεt deg yal axxam i yiḍ n 20 deg yebrir
neɣ  d  amezgun  neɣ  d  kra  n  ccna  i  d-yesmektayen 
Yal  aseggas  mi  ara  d-yezzi  usmekti  n  tefsut  n  80 
tixnanasin  n  udabu  azzayri,  i  yezgan  ibedd  mgal 
akked  tefsut  taberkant  n  2001,  tamurt  n  Leqbayel 
n  tutlayt  d  tumast  tamaziɣt,  am  akken  sqerdicen 
akken  ma  tella  ttbaddaden  ɣer  usmekti-ines  akken 
tamsalt n tumast d tutlayt ɣer wanda i telḥeq d acu 
iwata, acku d ayen ur yezmir ad yettu yiwen, d ayen 
i  mazal  ilaqen  ad  yettusutar  d  wamek  i  yettaεraḍ 
ur nezmir ad yettwamḥu acku d yiwen n uḥric yesεan 
udabu ad ibedd mgal waya deg yal taswiεt.
azal meqqren deg umezruy-nneɣ.

Meɣres  1980  mi  id  as  ugin  i  umaru  ameqqran

di  tesdawit  n  Tizi  Wezzu  akken  ad  yemmeslay

Kader Belaidi,
Aselmad n Tmaziɣt 
deg Uẓeffun

«I kunwi ay ayetma n umennuɣ 
n tinzert, I kemm d kečč, i kunwi 
ur nessin tuggdi, i kunwi a wid 
facal deg-sen yeɣli, i kunwi 
a wid yessaramen ma ɣlin ad 
uɣalen d idɣaɣen gar yifassen 
n wayetmaten-nsen yis-sen ad 
reǧǧmen imesfessden n udabu n 
lɛaṛ, adabu i d-yewwin aẓar seg 
uḥarki. I kunwi ay Imaziɣen ,a 
wid ur nbeddel adrum s waɣrum, 
imi aɣrum nwen d amennuɣ ɣef 
tinzert d tlelli, I kunwi…
Awal-iw ,ad wen-t-in-azneɣ, 
ma cḍaɣ deg-s surfet–iyi. i 
kunwi yaɣlin deg yirebbi n 
udabu amesbaṭṭli, yerrakken deg 
unekraf n Tizi , seg-mi i tugim 
tizelgi, tugim ad tenzem s ulac 
di tmurt-nwen ad tecbum inebgi. 
Tugim ad tsiǧwem idamen n 
yimaɣrasen n tlelli, Imaɣrasen 
n tmanyin i isaɣli umesbaṭṭli, 
tugim ad tsiǧwem idammen n 
ugar n meyya uɛecrin d ilemẓi, 
tafsut taberkant cfut-as , neɣ 
alset-tt i wid ur d-necfi, deg-s 
tamurt n Leqbayel tekker-d, 
temlal teqbaylit d uqbayli. 
Kunwi, tugim ad teddum d 
iqfafen d wid yenzan s ukarsi, 
ddan d irbiben s ičumar, lɛaṛṛ 
nawlen-t d imensi, i wegdud 
dewṛen aɛrur, tirrugza deg-
sen ur telli. A weltma, a gma, 
tugim tikerkas, tugim tixidas, 
tugim timenqas. Ih, tugim ddel, 
tugim asmundel, tugim aḥerkel. 
Tewwim abrid n tjeddit , abrid 
i d-yenǧeṛ jedd-nwen Masnsen 
d Yugurten, abrid n yimarawen 
yettujarden ger tezrigin n 
Yimaziɣen. Cacnaq ,yessenger 
Farɛun, Aksil yemmuger 
Ɛuqqba, Ɛebban, Krim , Buḍyaf, 
Si Lḥusin, Ɛmiṛuc d waṭṭas n 
niḍen sufɣen Fṛensis. Ǧawut, 
Mɛemmri, Busebsi d waṭṭaaaas 
i yettwanɣen, bedden s tira-nsen 
sdat ijenwiyen n yirebraben.
Kunwi ay ayetma ass-a, 
tbeggsem agus n tissas, tabɣest 
deg wen tettnarni, tefkam lɛahd 
i tyimmatin i iwalan tarwa-nsent 
taɣli, jarḥent ,qudrent taswin-
nsent, kunwi tegrem-asent 
irebbi, s amennuɣ tegrem iman-
nwen , melba akukru ,melba 
tuggdi, temmugrem acangal n 
lmut  n yimḍebbren ihemmjen d 
tirni, adabu iswi-s iban ,ur yeǧǧi 
isem n yilelli. Maca, tirga-s fɣent 
mxalfa, mi tbeddem ɣef tizi n 
Tizi, yiwen wawal i tecnam, 
ulaaac smaḥ d wigi, wiyyi i 
wen-yeɣzan tasraft, ttṛajun deg-s 
ad taɣlim , kunwi  ur  tecciḍem 
ara, d abrid n tezdeg i tewwim. 
Ay ayetma , ɣas ur ttaysem ara, 
ittij-nwen ad d-yeflali ,tafsut 
fell-awen ad d tefsu s yizeǧǧigen 
n tayri, tayri ad tsali azeṭṭa ger

deg-s surfem-iyi, rriɣ kan ad

asirem rret  -tt d iswi.»

Tafsut n 81 deg Bgayet
Ɣas  tuget  n  wid  yellan  deffir  n 
yebrir  80,  amennuɣ  ur  yerkid 
ara,  inejmuɛen  ur  ḥbisen  ara,

sya  awal 
deg  Tizi, 
rran-d 
seg  Summam.

Bgayet, imi deg lawan-nni Bgayet 
urɛad

i  tikli  i  wass  n  19  deg  mayyu.

tin  Bgayet  s  yijeǧǧigen  d  ccna.

Llan  ula  d  wid  iwmi  ḥekmen  ar

Tafsut taberkant 
Tafsut imaziɣen rnu-as timenɣiwt 
n  unaẓur,  n  ubabat,  n  umedya 
n  yiqbayliyen  merra  Lwennas 
Maɛtub,  annect-agi  akk  mazal 
urɛad  teḥli  cama-is,  mazal  lǧerḥ 
d  ajdid,  tiyita  mačči  d  tin  ara 
yettwatun,  atan  daɣen  tuɣal-d 
tmḥeqranit  i  tikkelt  tis  meyya 
mgal  agdud  aqbayli,  tikkelt-agi 
d  tarwiḥt  n  yilemẓi  Massinissa 
Germaḥ  i  iruḥen  d  asfel,  imi  ur 
yeqbil ara tamuḥqranit n yiwen n 
uqcic dɣa reffdent yimsulta n At 
Dwala,  wwtent  s  rrṣaṣ  armi  id-
as  sxarben  ṣṣura-is,  Massinissa 
wwint  ɣer  sbiṭar  n  Tizi-Uzzu, 
syin  akkin  imi  tesɛeb  liḥala-is 
wwint  ɣer  Lezzayer  tamanaɣt, 
dɣa  dinna  id  d-tessawel  lmut 
tewwi 
tarwiḥt-is,  arrac  n  At 
Dwala  imi  i  ten  yiweḍ  lexbar, 
mmsefhemen akken ulac tuɣalin 
ɣer  deffir,  ṭṭfen  di  rray-nsen, 
ttar  n  Massinissa  ad  d-yuɣal, 
nnejmaɛent tudrin, ilmeẓyen ṭṭfen 
abrid akken ad sbegnen i umaḍal 
d akken tamuḥqranit tɛedda tilas, 
kra nnan-as Massinisa d yiwen i 
yettakren, ur yelli ara d anelmad, 
dɣa  tawacult,  imezdaɣ  n  tuddar, 
inelmaden  n  tesnawiyin  d  wid 
i  iɣaḍ  lḥal,  am  yiwen  n  urgaz 

bbaɛzqen-d  si  tudrin,  ččuren-d 
iberdan,  ffɣen  ttsuɣun  :  “ulac 
smaḥ,  ulac”.  Ṣṣut  i  d-yeffɣen 
seg  Wat  Dwala  yeṭṭerḍeq  di  yal 
taddart ffɣen-d.
Aṭas n yilmeẓyen i iruḥen d asfel 
di  teswiɛt-nni,  yal  taddart  tesɛa 
ameɣras, yal tawacult tettwajraḥ, 
mmuten azal n 128 n yilmeẓyen, 
taswiɛt tessaweḍ ɣef ulac tuɣalin 
ɣef deffir.
Imenɣi  ɣef  yidles  akked  tutlayt 

tamaziɣt deg Lzayer d aqdim, si 
zik mi yella, tutlayt-agi aṭas i umi 
tettaqraḥ di tɛabbuṭ, aṭas i umi id 
d-tella  d  aɛewwiq,  wissen  ayen. 
Agdal  ar  ass  n  wass-a  mazal-it 
yettkemil,  kunwi  teẓram  nekkni 
neẓra.

ɣef 

Ulɣu. Akabar n Agraw n Yidles 
d  Tugdud  d  win  yuɣen  tanumi 
yettemeslay-d 
tedyanin 
yeḍran  deg  tefust  n  yebrir  n  80 
neɣ ulama d win n tfsut tabarkant, 
imi akabar n RCD d win d-sllulen 
kra  n  yimaɣnassen  yellan  d 
asaḍen  deg  talit n  80  anida  fkan 
udem amaynut i tsartit, wten deg 
yal  tamiwin  ad  seḥbibren  ɣef 
yeswi  i  ɣef  ɣlin  tarwiḥi,  ladɣa 
tid  n  yimaɣrassen  n  tegrawla  n 
54,  wid  yenuḍḥen  ɣef  tezzayrit 
tazzirit wid yessarmen ad idirren 
deg tegmat d tuget n yidelsan neɣ 
n tutlayin tesɛa tmurt-nneɣ.
Akabar  n  RCD,  ass-a  yesseḍfar 
awal  tigawt,  imi  yura-d  ulɣu  s 
tmaziɣt d tajmilt i wid akk yefkan 
iman-sen  d-iseflan  ɣef  tutlayt-a, 
iwakken ad segzin tilufa d iḥulfan 
yesɛa ukabar-a ɣer tama n tutlayt 
n  tmaziɣt  d  umezruy-is  lqayen. 
Ɛerḍen  fkan-d  kra  n  tiktiwin  ɣef 
umezruy  yefren  d  tid  nettɛic 
ass-a,  imi  deg  ulɣu-nsen,  nnan 
d  akken  yebrir  80  d  win  yewten 
iẓuran-is  alama  d  tegrawla  n 
54,  yella-d  d  timlilit  ger  tsuta 
ɣef  yiwen  n  yeswi  ladɣa  win  n 
tlelli  yettwaksen  seld  timunent 
Lezzayer.

daɣ

n usmekti i useggas-a, ɣas ulama 
d wid yuɣen tannumi imi asmekti 
n  tefsut  imaziɣen  d  tin  n  2001 
tekcem  deg  wansayen  n  ukabar. 
Taswiɛt tettidir talsa ur tesumaḥ.
Imi  d-wwin  awal  ɣef  unfafad 
n  covid-19,  fursen  taswiɛt  rran 
tajmilt  i  yal  wid  ixeddmen  deg 
uḥric n tezmert ɣas ulama s lqella 
n  ttawilat,  imi  tizemmar-nsen 
d  tid  yettqaballen  amahi  udem 
allen,  akken  ur  yettu  ara  wid  i 
asen-d-igan  tiwizi  deg  teswiɛt-a 
n  leḥris  ladɣa  tidukla  n  ugraw 
mgal covid-19, ayen iwmi qqaren 
s trumit “Stop Covid-19”.
Γer  taggara,  akabar  RCD  d  win 
yewwten  s  leqsaḥ  deg  tsertit  n 
udabu,  yekkaten  ad  yessemɣi 
tugdi  gar  yimeɣnasen  n  Ḥirak. 
Ifures  udabu  taswiɛt  n  ukman, 
yerfed aṭas ɣer leḥbus.Sawalen-d 
i  userreḥ  n  yal 
ameɣnas 
yettuḥebsen  ɣef  tikti-s  neɣ  ɣef 
tmagit-is.

RCD  yesmekta-d  akken  abrid

d-wekden ɣer tagara n ulɣu-nsen.

TAFSUT N 80

03

Asmekti
D awezɣi ad nettu 
tafsut n 80

Ccfaya. Deg wayyur n meɣres, 
deg useggas n 1980, tella-d 
yiwet n tedyant, anda amussnaw, 
amedyaz, amaru ameqqran n 
tmurt n Yimaziɣen, Mouloud 
Mammeri neɣ akken i yuɣ 
isem deg tmurt n Leqbayel Dda 
Lmulud, yebna ad d-yexdem 
asarag ɣef tmedyezt taqbaylit 
taqburt. Asarag i t-id-iheyyan 
d Tasqamut n Yisdawanen n 
Tesdawit n Tizi-Wezzu. Maca 
wid i d-yefrurin seg tikta n At 
Ḥemdu d At Tɛerbubt yellan deg 
tqacuct n leḥkem n lawan-nni, 
wid yeswan seg taεwint n ddel 
d lbaṭel, wid i ɣeḍlen atmaten-
nsen, ma mazal tettamnem yes-
sen ; ɣas sersen ɣef tuyat-nwen 
itran, nnan-d ala, geden asarag, 
ur qbilen tikta yemxalfen tid-
nsen. 
Argaz neɣ d tameṭṭut seg temẓi 
i ttnaɣen mgal adabu bu tkerkas 
yenɣan asirem n tmurt akken d 
aleqqaq. Agdud aqbayli yufa-tt 
d tawaɣit ahat yesɛan leslaḥ ara 
yekksen akk iserbas n yimsulṭa 
deg tudrin n Leqbayel. Ɛewlen 
ɣef lbaṭel ad t-kksen, ɛewlen 
ɣef leḥqara ad tt-nedlen. Ihi, 
xelqen-d Leqbayel yiwen n 
umussu ara yennaɣen mgal 
aya, d amussu adeksan amaziɣ 
i d-yessawalen yal tikkelt ɣer 
tmesbanit ara d-yini awal-is deg 
tlemmast n Lezzayer tamanaɣt. 
Ad suɣen s yiwen n ssut ala 
i lbaṭel, dayen i temḥeqranit 
deg tmurt n tmazɣa. Neɛya 
seg txidas n udabu yettnuɣun 
ilmeẓyen am yizan. Anwa ara 
yettun ass yecban ass am wa 20 
deg yebrir asmi yekker uɣebbar, 
yekker dduxxan deg tlemmast n 
tmurt n Leqbayel.

Nacer Akouche

Sɣur  Tahar Ould Amar

Werǧin ad d-tuɣal tekmamt i tefsut

Uqbel ad teffeɣ 
Fransa, yuɣ 
lḥal aṭas seg 
yilmeẓyen-
nni n umussu 
aɣelnaw i nɣan. 
Tajmilt i Benai, 
Laimeche, 
Rachid Ali Yahia, 
Ould Hamouda, 
Henine, 
Ouseddik, 
Oubouzar, 
Belhocine 
Hadjres… 

Asmekti wis 40 n Tefsut n Yimaziɣen akked wis 19 n 
Tefsut Taberkant, yaf-aɣ-d nekmen deg yixxamen. Meɛna, 
coronavirus ur yessaweḍ ara ad yerr tikmamin akked leqyud 
i Tefsut akken tent-yerra i “youm lɛilm”. Cfawat llant-d di 
ttiɛad, seg ddurt iɛeddan. Azeṭṭa n facebook yuɣal d Tafsut, 
yal ta, yal wa yezzuzur deg-s tajmilt, tanagit. Azeṭṭa isaḥ-d 
i 127 n yilemẓyen n wassaɣ yeɣlin d asfel, imeḥbas n 
Berwagiya n 80 akked tcemmuɛin i terwiḥin n yimeɣnasen-
imeɣrasen. 
Yenna Said Sadi deg wawal-is i Tiɣremt : « tarwa n 80 
tessekcem asirem ar wul, tessers tugdut deg walaɣ ». Ad as-
nernu arrac n 80 mlan abrid n tifrat i tsuta d-iteddun, akken 
s-nemlan abrid imenza n umussu aɣelnaw. Ulamek nɛedda d 
abrid ɣef yimezwura deg umezruy n Lezzayer i sebblen iman-
nnsen akken ad rren laṣel i laṣel-is. Di tallit-nni, iseggasen 
40, llan d takemmict n yilmeẓyen i yugin asfunteḥ n Messali 
Hadj. D imezwura yezzuzren tikti n “ma ulac tamaziɣt, ulac, 
ulac...”. Tikti-nsen ur tuɣ ara, ur tuɣ ara ula gar “watmaten”. 
Qqaren-asen “mačči d lawan. Mi teffeɣ Fransa…”. Uqbel ad 
teffeɣ Fransa, yuɣ lḥal aṭas seg yilmeẓyen-nni n umussu 
aɣelnaw i nɣan. Tajmilt i Benai, Laimeche, Rachid Ali Yahia, 
Ould Hamouda, Henine, Ouseddik, Oubouzar, Belhocine 
Hadjres… Ṭṭaqa seg-sen wwḍen leɛfu Rebbi. Teɣzi n leɛmer i 
Rachid Ali Yahia akked Sadek Hadjres.
Si 1980 ar ass-a, yal aseggas rezzunt-d tefsutin di yebrir. 
Smektayent-aɣ-d belli urɛad d-nḥella Tafsut-nni yebɣa wul, 
bɣan lejwareḥ. Di Tuber 88, rfan yilmeẓyen, ffɣen-d s iberdan. 
Ass-nni, neḍmeɛ d tikta n 80 d-yennulfan deg waṭas n 
temnaḍin n Tmurt. Asirem, ndan-as tifexxet At Ḥemdu, rran 
Tamurt d zawiya. Rran ẓẓerb i tirga, asirem, tilelli, tugdut, … 
Imeɣnasen imagdayen ur zmiren ad beddlen taswiɛt i yiman-
nsen, imi agdud yexsa, iruḥ am win izeṭlen. Tegra-d cwiṭ n 
Tmurt n Leqbayel tettnaḍaḥ. Anaḍeḥ-nni yefreq isertayen n 
temnaḍt am yibawen ɣef lluḥ. Nenna dayen, tikkelt-a tegrareb 
Lezzayer.
Am akken d targit, di Furar 2019, yeffeɣ ugdud i yiman-is, 
ulac win s-yeṭṭfen afus, tewweḍ-it-id tiɣri n 80, yessutur 
tilelli akken tt-sutren warrac n Tefsut. Yerna-yas : « Casbah, 
Bab el Oued d imaziɣen! ». Ɣas akka kemnen warrac n Bab-
Lwad, asirem ur yekmin ara… Ma ur d-telli ara txazabit akked 
tfexxet, targit n 80 ad tt-tessufeɣ tsuta n 2000. Ma qṭan-as 
abrid tikelt-a, … d taqsiṭ-nniḍen.

T. O. A.

TAFSUT N 80

04
Seg tefsut n 80 ar ass-a

Ilemẓiyen.  Inelmaden-a  i  d-yeffɣen  deg  wass  n  20  deg  yebrir  ɣas 
ttwaḥebsen, xelsen tilelli n wawal i ɣef ttnaɣen s tecraḍ ur nttekkes...

yesɛan azal ɣer yimaziɣen, 
tumert  d 
ttmagaren-tt  s

acḥal  n  tikkal  i  teqqel  tefsut-a  d

yid-sen,  maca  amezruy  ad  inagi 
fell-asen, d imenza i yegren lsas

Gar  useggas  n  94  d  95  arrac  n

uḥebbus  d  ubelleɛ  n  yiɣerbazen,

n  udabu  s  uzref  n  yimaziɣen  d

n  yiɣerbazen  i  deg  tt-selmaden,

i  yeǧǧan  axeddim-nsen  uɣalen 
ɣer uselmed n tmaziɣt, selmaden 
tikwal  deg  wugar  n  kraḍ  n 
yiɣerbazen,  iswi-nsen  mačči  d 
tadrimt neɣ d ayen-nniḍen, iswi-
nsen ad siwḍen ad seɣren tamaziɣt 
i wamur ameqqran n yinelmaden 
n temnaḍt-a.  Deg useggas n 1998 
teqqel-d  temnaḍt-a  ur  nḥebbes 
amennuɣ  ɣer  yiberdan,  tamnaḍt

d 

qaren.  Ulac  tugdut-nni  ḥala  deg

TAFSUT N 80

05

Dr Said Sadi i uyalas Tiɣremt deg usmekti n Tefsut n 80
«Tafsut n 80 tettalas-aɣ tidet.
Tidet-agi, tettalas-aɣ-tt diɣen tarwa-nneɣ.»
Tafsut. Tirga n Lezzayer n tegmat, sawlen fell-as yimeɣnasen n 49. Ḥaca wid yesfuṛuyen 
tillas iwakken ad sinifen tagrawla i yeqqaren tanekra-ya ur tesɛi imawlan, ur tesɛi aẓar. 
Bɣan ad tt-rren d tarbibt, akkenni ad as-keḥlen amek i sen-yehwa. 49, 56, 80 d tliwa 
ideg i d-tugem tegrawla n furar 2019. Ass n 27 duǧember tamdint n Lezzayer terfed s 
umata tteswiṛa n Ɛebban Remḍan.

tilellit 

40 n yiseggasen i Lezzayer 

Tamagdayt 
; 
lḥekkam  ttemsetbaɛen 
wa  deffir  wa  yiwen  ur  d-slin.  Tikti 
ur  tessaweḍ  ara,  mačči  d  abrid  i 
tfernem ur nlaq ? Neɣ ahat, d agdud 
ur d-neḍfir deg lawan ?
Yal  yiwen  d  acu  iɣef  yettnadi,  yal  yiwen 
amek  i  yettwali  amennuɣ  di  tsertit. Yella 
ukersi, tella tugdut. Yella win yettnadin ad 
yeṭṭef amkan udabu neɣ amkan deg udabu. 
Yella win yekkaten ad d-yessali tiɣri n tlelli 
deg ugdud. Win yebɣan ad yuɣal d aqerru 
ɣas  akken  di  lbaṭel,  ɣur-s  sin  n  yiberdan 
: yezmer ad yeqleb tamurt akken xedmen 
wid  itt-yudin  ɣef  yiɣil,  yezmer  diɣen  ad 
isenteḍ  iman-is  ar  wid  ixenqen  agdud. 
Ma  d  win  yefkan  tameẓẓuɣt  i  wenza 
n  umezuy,yeḥsa  tidet  ɣezzif  umecwaṛ 
yessufuɣen tirga ar tafat. 
Lemmer  yemmut  Mandela  di  lḥebs,  aṭas 
ara s-yinin amennuɣ-ines yefsi, yeɣli deg 
yilem.
Amedya-nniḍen.  Asmi  nḥettem  ɣef 
Bouteflika ad  ibeddel lsas  n  lakul,  tikti n 
ccreɛ d udem n ddewla, ɣas akken yenna-d 
yeqbelcceṛt-nwen,  ɣas  akken  nessaweḍ-it 
armi i d-yefka awal zdat ugdud, ur kcimeɣ 
ara  nekk  s  yiman-iw  ar  leḥkem,  ulama  i 
mennaɣ  ad  iliɣ  ar  yidis-is.  Nenna-yas  ad 
nemwali  aseggas  neɣ  sin,  ma  teṭṭfeḍ  deg 
wawal-ik  ad  nkemmel  abrid  ɣef  wayen 
iɣef  nemsefham,  ma  tukreḍ  taqejjirt,  yal 
wa aqerruy-is di tcacit-is.
Yezmer  bab-is  ad  yesseḥseb 
tasertit 
akken-niḍen.  Kra  n  wayen  yellan  di 
tsertit 
tamagdayt  ass-a,  deg  yisufar-

i  d-frurin…  Anwa  i  s-yennan  ad  tili

ur  nerji  agdud,  weḥd-s,  yekker-d 
ad  yekkes  leḥkem  aɛsekri.  Amek 
i  tettwaliḍ  tanekra  n  furar  imi  deg 
udlis i d-turiḍ Tegrawla tesxedmem 
awal “Miracle” ? Nezmer ad nefhem 
ur tt-truǧam ara ?
Nekk  s  yiman-iw,  uriɣ-d 
tabrat  deg 
uɣmis  n  Liberté,  kra  n  wussan  uqbel 
tanekra,  anida  d-nniɣ  ulamek  ara  teqqim 
tegnit  akken  tella. Awal-agi  n  “Miracle”, 
nniɣ-t-id  ɣef  wakken  d  ilmeẓyen  yakk  d 
tilawin  i  d-yezwaren  ar  ubrid.  Ilmeẓyen 
yesderɣel-iten  lakul,  tilawin  yurez-itent 
lqanun. D wid-nni i yenwa udabu gugmen 
i  d-yendekwalen  d  imenza. Akken  yebɣu 
yili, tanekra-agi n furar ur d-teɣli ara deg 
yigenni.  Amennuɣ  n  talwit  werǧin  yella 
di  tsersit  tazzayrit  uqbel  80.  Nekni  diɣen 
nesqucceḍ-d  ar  wid  iɣ-yezwaren.  Awal 

Tagrawla n furar 2019, i yezgan deg 
ukman  ussan-a,  tegla-d  s  usirem 
meqqren.  Ahat  ad  yekmen  usirem 
ula d netta asmi ara d-yaweḍ lawan 
n  usqerdec  n  temsal  tigejdanin  n 
Lezzayer n uzekka yecban : amkan 
n ddyana, izerfan n tmeṭṭut, tamagit, 
atg.  Nwala  yakan  El  Badissia  deg 
unnar  d-ijebden  ar  tama-s  amur 
ameqqran  n  ugdud.  Ar  taggara,  ur 
d-yewwiḍ  ara  lawan  ad  yesteɛref 
yiwen  s  Lezzayer  mm  yigduden 
yemxallafen s ara yebnu uwanek n 
uzekka ?
Ad  nettmeslay  ad  nettemsefham.  Awal 
d  taɣawsa  n  tsertit.  Ineslem  weḥd-s, 
amselman  d  ayen-nniḍen.  Tagi  d  yiwet. 
Tis  snat,  ur  nessemnennay  ara  amagday 
yeqqaren bɣiɣ ad d-iniɣ awal-iw di tmurt-

«Tarwa  n  80  tessekcem  asirem  ar  wul, 
tessers 
Iwakken 
tugdut  deg  wallaɣ. 
agdud ad yesbedd adabu ara yefken azal 
i yizerfan-ines, ilaq ayen yellan d amenni 
ad yuɣal d idles n tsertit.»

megdal  leḥkem  aɛsekriw,  di  Ṣummam,i 
d-ilul deg useggas n 56. Tirga n Lezzayer 
n  tegmat,  sawlen  fell-as  yimeɣnasen  n 
49.  Ḥaca  wid  yesfuṛuyen  tillas  iwakken 
ad  sinifen  tagrawla  i  yeqqaren  tanekra-
yagi ur tesɛi imawlan, ur tesɛi aẓar. Bɣan 
ad  tt-rren  d  tarbibt,  akkenni  ad  as-keḥlen 
amek i sen-yehwa. 49, 56, 80 d tliwa ideg 
i  d-tugem  tegrawla  n  furar  2019.  Ass  n 
27 duǧember tamdint n Lezzayer terfed s 
umata tteswiṛa n Ɛebban Remḍan.
Teqqim-d  taluft  n  wid  yeɣran  am  akka 
teqqareḍ.  D  tidet,  amur  ameqqran  ddurin 
agdud, ttrajun anda ara tmil, d acu ara ten-
id-isaḥen… Di yebrir 80, wid d-yezwaren 
: wa d aselmad di tsedawit, wa d amejjay, 
wa  d  ajenyuṛ,  wa  d  analmad. Ass-a,  wid 
irefden iman-nsen di tmeddurt-nsen uɣalen 
am  akken  kukran  abeddel.  Ameɣnas-nni 
yettakken  abeḥri  i  turin  akken  s-yenna 
Lwennas,  yuɣal  yekkat  s  tayet  amek  ara 
yekcem  ar  ugraw  aɣelnaw,  neɣ  ad  yeṭṭef 
taɣiwant. Asmi d-yenna ugdud, di meɣres 

iw,  dacu  kan  lsas  n  tugdut  am  tlelli  n 
umeslay, izerfan n umdan, azal gar urgaz d 
tmeṭṭut, asinef n ddin ɣef tsertit… yiwen ur 
ten-itekkes… d umeslman yeqqaren tilleli 
d  nekk  ara  s-yeggen  tilas;  ma  ufrareɣ-d 
di  tefranin,  rray  d  rray-iw,  awal  d  awal-
iw.  El  Badissiya,  teccelqef tagrawla n  54 
iɣef terwel di tazwara, tura tebɣa diɣen ad 
tesberber  ɣef  tin  n  furar  2019.  Ddin  deg 
umkan-is,  tasersit  ɣur-s  abrid-is.  Ass-a, 
tikti-yagi attan ters-dar unnar. Ilaq ad as-
neqqim. Ma ur nefri ara tagi, acemma ur 
aɣ-d-yettban.  Amxalefn  tekta  ur  yelli  d 
ugur,  fell-as  i  tebna  tugdut.  Adt-neqqar 
iḍ  d  wass  :  tugdut  mačči  kan  d  tifranin, 
tugdut  ɣur-s  lsas.  Yal  win  yessawalen  s 
yisem-is, ilaq-as ad yeḥsu ur yezmir ara ad 
yesserwet beṛṛa n unnar.

Telliḍ gar wid yellan deffir n 20 deg 
yebrir.  Kečč  d  yirfiqen-ik  txelsem 
tikkin-nwen deg Tefsut n Yimaziɣen 
s leḥbus d yidim. Seg zik, amennuɣ-
inek ɣef Lezzayer Tilellit Tamagdayt 
ara ireṣṣin tikli deg unnar n yizerfan 
d  tlelliyin  yemgarden  ladɣa  wid 
yerzan  tamagit.  40  n  yiseggasen 
mbeɛd, ad d-yeḍru waya s tidet deg 
tmetti ma yessaweḍ ibeddel unhil ?
Leqdic  umi  d-neqqim  meqqer.  Yenna-
yas  “lecɣal  n  taddart  meqqrit,  nekni 
nekker-d  mezziyit”.  Iwakken  ad  d-tuɣal 
Tmazɣa  ar  umezruy-ines,  s  wudem-ines, 
amecwaṛ  ad  yeɣzif.  Tamaziɣt  tezmer 
ad  tili  tameslayt  n  tussna  d  uzal  di  kra  n 
yiseggasen. Ameslay  ttun  Leqbayel,  atan 
ar Yimẓabiyen, win i ulac-it di Lezzayer, 
yella  di  Lmerruk,  ayen  yeṣfeḍ  umezruy 
deg  Tferka  Ugafa  atan  ar  Twareg... 
Iwakken  ad  nessali  leqdic  am  wagi,  tlaq 
tedrimt, laqent tɣawsiwin n ddewla. Llan 
yigduden, amwin n Finland, i d-yeskeflen 

Yettkemmil deg sb. 06

«Asmi d-yenna ugdud, di meɣres akked 
yebrir 2019, d lawan ad nessali tasawent 
di talwit i udadu-yagi ma nebɣa ad d-yefk 
tameẓẓuɣt,  d  wid-nni  umi  d-tewwi  ad 
zwiren i yeskawen ifadden i uɣref.»

Deg  useggas  n  80,  imussnawen 
ddant  ar  yidis  n  ugdud,  “widen 
yeɣran mmlan i yimeɣban”, i s-yenna 
Matoub.  40  n  yiseggasen  mbeɛd, 
amur ameqqran seg yimussnawen-a 
beddlen  tayett  i  tmekḥelt,  lḥan  d 
ljerra  n  leḥkem.  Furar  2019,  yiwen 

akked  yebrir  2019,  d  lawan  ad  nessali 
tasawent di talwit i udadu-yagi ma nebɣa 
ad  d-yefk  tameẓẓuɣt,  d  wid-nni  umi 
d-tewwi  ad  zwiren  i  yeskawen  ifadden  i 
uɣref. D acu kan, asmi walan yinelmaden, 
imeqranen-nsen unafen, cleqfen tiɣri n 80 
leqmen-tt ɣef tegrawla.

Deg  yiwet  n  tdiwennit  tefkiḍ  i  Le

Ayen  yellan  d  amecwar-inu  deg-s  3  n

d-yeffeɣ anebdu-yagi. Ma d tira ɣef Tefsut

ɣef  ugerruj-agi,  ad  t-nsemlil  iwakkan  ad

is, yesfeḍ kra n wid ukud ur temselḥuy ara 
ass-a. Tafsut  n  80  tettalas-aɣ  tidet. Tidet-
agi, tettalas-aɣ-tt diɣen tarwa-nneɣ.

Yiwen seg yimyura i nettraju ad nɣer 
s teqbaylit d Dr Sadi. Ur tebniḍ ara 
ad d-ternuḍ kra i tsekla n tmaziɣt ?
Tura  la  ferneɣ  gar  tira  n  nnig  50  n 
yiseggasen n umennuɣ. Aṭas n leqdic. Mi 
terked  tegnit,  wissen  ad  d-nestafi  i  tira  s 
tmaziɣt.  Neṭṭef  igenni  tamurt  :  tafat  ɣef 
umezruy, ameyyez ɣef tegrawla, asekfel n 
tira n zik, timliliyin... D acu kan, d tidet, 
yezwar ṭɛam taẓalit. Lemmer d lebɣi, tira s 
tmaziɣt, ad tt-nettawi d aɛwin.

n umennuɣ ɣef tmagit

Azamul. D tanekra mgal wi yebɣan ad aɣ-snegren aẓar n tmuzɣa di 
tmurt n tmazɣa. Wid yeqqaren akken taluft-a n tmaziɣt d tmagit mačči 
d lweqt-is ! Ad asen-nini i kunwi anwi i d lweqt-nwen ?

Karim Sɛawi

«Amennuɣ ur ifuk ara. Ahat d tagrawla n 22 furar…»

Tiɣremt  ur  yesɛi  ara  assaɣ  d  tira  neɣ 
leqwanen.  Lukan  d  asekkil  n  taɛrabt  i 
d  aɣbel,  d  acu  i  ten-yeṭṭfen  akken  ad 
d-suffɣen  aɣmis  yuran  s  taɛrabt.  Ala, 
ssebba mačči d ta. Ssebba n sseḥ d karuh 
n  tmagit  tamaziɣ,  acḥal  n  lesnin  aya. 
Ssarameɣ-awen  afud  igerrzen,  ḥsut,  aqli 
beddeɣ ɣer yidis-nwen. Send iḍelli, ssebt 
yezrin  nemmekta-d  tamettant  n  Guermah 
Massinissa  deg  uxxam  n  yiğadarmiyen 
n At  Dwala  akked  127  d  ilemẓi  yeɣlin  d 
asfel  di Tefsut Taberkant. Ad  rreɣ  tajmilt 
i  yilmeẓyen-a  yefkan 
tirwiḥin-nsen 
ɣef  tmaziɣt.  Ur  tettuɣ  ara  imeyyaten  n 
yimejraḥ.  S  yidammen-a  i  yebda  leḥkem 
n  Bouteflika. Ar  ass-a  tamurt  n  Leqbayel 
ur tesfiḍ ara imeṭṭawen-is. Wid d-yellan d 
ssebba n lmut n warrac-nneɣ, kar deg-sen 
ha-ten-an  ass-a  deg  leḥkem,  yezmer  llan 
gar-asen widen yugin ad tili Tiɣremt.
Ad  d-uɣaleɣ  s  asteqsi-inek.  Di  yebrir 
80,  tuɣ-iyi  d  aselmad  deg  tesdawit  n 
Bab  Ezzouar  i  yeldin  di  74  (aseggas-
iw  aneggaru).  Imir,  USTHB  llan  deg-s 
tamanaɣt 
yinelmaden 
akked  wid  n  tmurt  n  Leqbayel.  D  aya  i 
yeǧğan  tasdawit  n  Bab  Ezzouar  d  annar 
tamaziɣt.  Deg  useggas 
n 
amezwaru  nessended-d 
tirebbuyaɛ  n 
ccna  akked  umezgun.  Nekk,  lliɣ  ttekkiɣ 
di  terbaɛt  Tagrawla,  mazal-itt  dɣa  ar 
ass-a.  Nettheyyi-d  timliliyin  tidelsanin, 
tisertanin.  Ttekkin  deg-sen  yimdukkal-
nneɣ n Fac Centrale, n Ben Aknoun akked 
Tizi-Wezzu. Imir i nesla s umnaɛ n usarag 
n Mɛemri akked wayen i d-iḍefren di Tizi. 
D Djamal Zenati akked Salah Boukrif (ad 

n  Lezzayer 

tmeɣnest 

t-yerḥem Rebbi) i aɣ-d-yessawḍen isallen. 
Imiren  dɣa  i  nefka  ttiɛad  i  yimdukkal  n 
Fac Centrale (Mustapha Bacha, Arezki Ait 
Larbi…)  akken  ad  nemcawar  ɣef  wayen 
ara  nexdem.  Nebda  s  usunded  (grève 
générale)  deg  Bab  Ezzouar.  Ccɣel-nni  ur 
yeshil  ara,  imi  “les  frères  musulmans” 
akked  yiselmaden 
ibeɛtiyen  suffɣen-d 
tuccar-nsen.  Meɛna  ur  neḥbis  ara, 
nessaweḍ  alarmi  nqenneɛ  (s  lemɛawna 
n  yimdukkal  n  Fac  Centrale)  merra 
inelmaden,  ula  d  aɛrabawalen.  Aḥbas  n 
24 n yimeɣnasen ur aɣ-yessefcel ara : Yal 
ass  d  tikliwin  akked  addud  di  Lezzayer 
tamanaɣt, tama n Fac Centrale, akken ad 
ttwaserḥen yimeḥbas. 
Imi  iyi-tettunefk  tegnit,  ad  d-rreɣ  tajmilt 
i  merra  imdukkal-iw  imeɣnasen  yewḍen 
leɛfu  n  Rebbi  :  Mustapha  Bacha,  Salah 
Boukrif, M. Rachedi d wiyaḍ merra.
Ass-a,  20  yebrir  2020,  zemreɣ  ad  d-iniɣ 
ɣas ayen i aɣ-yeḍran mačči drus, Tamaziɣt 
tuɣal-d s annar n umennuɣ. Asekcem-is di 
tmendawt  d  tikerkas.  Amennuɣ  ur  ifuk 
ara.  Ahat,  tagrawla  n  22  furar  2019,  ad 
tkemmel ayen i d-tebda tefsut n yimaziɣen.

Amek  tettwaliḍ  tagrawla  n  furar 
“ikemnen” ussan-a ?
Di  75  uriɣ  asefru  i  terbaɛt  Tagrawla, 
qqareɣ-as  :  “Mazal  tagrawla  ur  tekfi. 
Tayeḍ  deg-s  ad  tefruri.  Baba  di  tmenzut 
yeɣli.  Tis  snat  ad  teglu  yes-i.  Mmi  ad 
yissin  tilelli.  Ma  ulac  mmi-s  n  mmi”. 
Mi  ara  selleɣ  i  yilmeẓyen  n  “Lḥirak” 
ttsuɣun 
gezzuɣ 
anamek  n  usefru-inu.  58  iseggasen  seld 

“Istiqlal, 

istiqlal”, 

timunent,  agdud  yefhem  belli  tagrawla  n 
54 ɣer timunent n ugdud, beddlen-as abrid 
yimnekcamen n daxel imaynuten Leɛsker 
n Ouajda yeṭṭef amkan n lɛesker n Fransa 
akken ad ḥewṣen lɣella n tmurt, ad tt-bḍun 
d  yimnekcamen  iqdimen.  22  di  furar  d 
tiririt  n  ugdud  i  temḥeqranit  n  terbaɛt  n 
Bouteflika i yekksen sser ɣef yizzayriyen 
s tuɣzi n 20 iseggasen, seg wass amenzu i 
deg yeṭṭef leḥkem akken ad d-yerr ttar, ad 
yeɣḍel  tarbaɛt  it-iwexren  si  leḥkem  asmi 
yemmut dada-s Boumèdienne, di 1979.
22  di  furar  di  temlilit  akked  tfelsafit  n 
Tefsut  n  Yimaziɣen,  imi  sumata,  agdud, 
di yal tamnaḍt, akken bɣunt ilint tektiwin-
is,  yekker-d  ad  d-iḥelli  tamɛict  n  lḥerma 
akked  liser.  22  di  furar  yelmed  si  20  di 
yebrir  amennuɣ  s  talwit.  Si  54  yelmed 
tazwert n uɣarem ɣef userdas akked tdukli 
n  ugdud  ɣas  mxalafen  deg  tmeslayin, 
di 
tsertit.  Asmi  sḥermen  asenǧaq  n 
yimaziɣen,  bɣan  ad  ṛzen  taddukli  akken 
ad ḥekmen s lebɣi-nsen. Ass-a d awezɣi ad 
d-nini belli ad texsi tegrawla, ayen yebɣu 
yexdem-it  udabu.  Agdud  yeḥsa  belli  d 
taddukli-ines i d lğehd-is akken ad yerreẓ 
tirebbuyaɛ n udabu i yettmeččan gar-asen, 
ussan-a. Iger-d ayen yura, ayen isuɣ ugdud 
di tekliwin ad yuɣal d asafar n tmetti ara 
yessemlilen  merra  Izzayriyen.  Tiɣerɣert 
n  Soummam,  Ulɣu  n  umenzu  n  unbir, 
ittafttaren n MCB, si 80, zemren ad d-ilin 
d  awelleh  i  Lezzayer  tamaynut.  Ilaq  tura 
ad  as-neqqim  i  ttawilat  i  ilaqen  akken  ad 
nesnerni  d  ccan  n  usafar. Afud  igerrzen  i 
Tiɣremt. Yid-wen.

Yesteqsa-t :
Tahar Ould Amar

Tagrawla.  Uqbel  80  i  yebda  Mohand 
Amarouche  yettnaḍaḥ  akken  ad  iḥelli 
tugdut akked tlelli i tmurt-is. D yiwen seg 
wudmawen n MCB ur yezmir ad t-yenker 
umezruy.  Di  yebrir  80,  tuɣ-it  d  aselmad 
di  tesdawit  n  Bab  Ezzouar.  Tuɣ-it  daɣen 
d aɛeggal di terbaɛt Tagrawla. Seg wass-
nni  ar  ass-a,  ur  yeḥbis  amennuɣ.  Yella 
di ttiɛad n tegrawla n furar. Ur icuḥ ara s 
tektiwin ara yessiwḍen tagrawla ɣer lber n 
laman. Yemmeslay-aɣ-d ɣef yebrir d furar. 
Slet-as…

Ma  ulac  uɣilif  ad  ak-rreɣ  cwiṭ  ar 
deffir. Anda i k-tuɣ ass 20 di yebrir 
1980 ?

terbaɛt  n  Tiɣremt.  Tekrem  s  ucqirrew  i

Agzul ɣef tefsut n Yimaziɣen
Acu  i  d  Tafsut  n  Yimaziɣen  ? 
Yal  aseggas  yettezzi-d  akken 
tarwa-s  ad  t-tesfugel,  ad  as-terr 
azal. Acku d azemz yesɛan azal, 
yettuɣal-d s yiseɣ, syin i d-yebda 
ubrid.  Yejmeɛ-d  idles,  tutlayt, 
amennuɣ,  asirem  d  tmaziɣt.  D 
aggur n yebrir, yettwarfed s lḥir, 
sɣur  wid  ur  nettwexxir.  D  tafsut 
umaziɣ,  yesddukklen  Leqbayel. 
Deg  wazemz  yecban  wagi,  d 
tikliwin  deg  ubrid  s  usenǧaq  n 
tlelli,  d  isaragen,  d  ccnawi,  d 
timeɣriwin  d  lfuruḥ  i  d-yettilin 
deg yal tama. Tafsut n Yimaziɣen 

terṣaṣin  n  yiǧadarmiyen,  dɣa  d 
ayen  i  d-yeglan  s  tlalit  n  leɛruc, 
imi walan belli ulac kra n ukabar 
i d-yegren iman-is, neɣ i iɛerḍen 
ad yekki akken ad yessens timest-
agi yekren. 
Ass  n  14  yulyu,  tella-d  yiwet  n 
tikli  d  tameqqrant  ɣer  Lezzayer 
tamannaɣt,  deg-s  uran  aḍris 
d’El  Kseur», 
«Plate-torme 
i  uselway  n  Lezzayer 
imir-
nni  Ɛebdlɛaziz  Budefliqa,  am 
wakken  i  yugin  akk  cwer  d 
ubadu.  Ssutren  deg-s  tamaziɣt  d 
tutlayt taɣelnawt yerna d tunṣibt, 
asṭeɛref n tmagit tamaziɣt n tmurt 
n Lezzayer, ...artg. Tikli-agi, d tin 
yettwagedlen,  yerna  tegla-d  s 
wazal  n  ɛecra  n  wid  yemmuten, 
mebla wid ur nban ma ttwaḥebsen 
neɣ 
ttwanɣan,  dɣa  kra  deg-
sen  banen-d,  wa  yemmut,  wa 
di  sbiṭar  yettwajreḥ.  Tafsut-agi 
taberkant, d tin d-yeglan s 126  n 
lmeytin, mebla wid yettwajerḥen, 
yettwaɛegben,  ar  ass  n  wass-a 
ggran-d  d  imeɛḍar:  wa  d  aḍar 
yegzem, wa d iẓri yedderɣel, ula 
d asgujel tesgujel arrac meẓẓiyen.

tin

merra  teddukel  u  tekker  mgal 
tamḥeqranit-a  d  maḥyaf-a  ɣef

tmurt n Lezzayer segmi i d-tḥella 
timunent-is  deg  1962.  Llant-d

tmurt n Leqbayel akked Lezzayer 
tamanaɣt,  maca  tiririt  n  udabu

acku aṭas n wid yettwaṭṭfen d wid 
yettwawten  seg  yimesbaniyen. 
Ass n 20 di yebrir 1980, yella-d 
userreḥ n wid yettwaṭṭfen, akken 
daɣ i d-yella uɛiwed n usɛeddi n 
ukayad  n  lbak  i  tikkelt  tis  snat, 
tanemmirt  tettuɣal  i  tuddsa  n

i  yellan  tettnaḍaḥ  iman-is  deg 
unnar  lawan-nni.  Seg  yimir  ar 
ass-a,  yettwasfugel  wass  n  20 
yebrir  deg  tmurt  n  Leqbayel  d 
tirni, yal mi ara d-yeḥḍer, ttilit-d 
tfaskiwin  d  tmeɣriwin  n  ccna 
sɣur  tiddukliwin  tidelsanin.  D 
ass n lficṭa daɣen, imi iɣerbazen 
meddlen tiwwura-nsen deg wass 
yecban assen.

s teɣzi n tudert.

ilmawen  d  yedmarren  ɛeryan. 
Imaziɣen  xelsen  Tamaziɣt  d 
tutlayt taɣelnawt deg tmenḍawt n 
tmurt s 126 d imeɣras. Amennuɣ 
ur yekfi !
Ar ass-a, Tamaziɣt, di tmurt-ines 
am tmura i ɣ-ḍ-iqerben, ur telli d 
tunsibt. Nessarem, limer neqqar: 
“Mazal lxir ɣer zdat”.
neqqar: 
ad 
Maca  mazal 
“Amennuɣ  yettkemmil  ;  mazal 
fell-aɣ ur yekfi !”

yiseggasen 

Mohand Ait Ighil

Tiɣremt  -  Un 42   Arim 20 yebrir 2020

Adiwenni akked Arezki Aït-Larbi
Timmeɣnest. D tagnit iwakken ad refden akk iɛeggalen-nni i iqeddcen ɣef tumast d 
yidles  amaziɣ.  Nufa-d  iman-nneɣ  deg  22  deg  lḥebs  n  Lḥerrac.  Ḥekmen  fell-aɣ  deg 
Tuber 1981. 

Arezki Ait Larbi
Aneɣmas

Uqbel, ulac amek 
ara d-yini umaziɣ 
awal-is. ayen akk 
icudden ɣer temsalt 
n tmaziɣt temdel 
fell-as tewwurt. 
D ayen ara aɣ-
yeǧǧen, ad nessali 
deg ccan n umussu 
n 80 imi agdud 
icqarrew adabu i 
d-yeffɣen i lbaṭel 
ɛinani.

yella ula d aɣmis  i ttɛelliqen ɣef leḥyuḍ, 
qessiḥ mliḥ. Llant ula d timeɣriwin, ladɣa 
tid  ideg  icennu  Ferḥat  Imaziɣen  Imula  i 
yesɛeddayen tikti n umennuɣ ɣef tumast d 
yidles amaziɣ deg tesdawit.
Mačči  kan  da  i  neqqim,  maca  yal  tikkelt 
ara  tili  temlilit  ɣef  tsertit  tadelsant  ara 
d-iheyyi  FLN,  akabar  awḥid  i  yellan  deg 
lweqt-nni,  nettruḥu  iwakken  ad  d-nefk 
tikti-nneɣ i yiqeddacen n udabu. Ma nwala 
ur nzemmer ara ad nesɛeddi rray-nneɣ, ad 
newwet  amek  ara  nsexreb  anejmuɛ-nni  n 
FLN. 

I 

Ɛeddan  kra  n  wayyuren,  tban-d  temḍunt 
n  yizerfan  n  umdan,  ass  n  30  deg  yunyu 
1985. 
tmurt  n 
tikkelt-nniḍen  seg 
Leqbayel  i  d-tekka,  wid  i  tt-id-yesnulfan 
sɛeddan tidyanin n Yebrir 80. 
S  umennuɣ-a  ɣef  tumast,  tutlayt,  idles 
akked  tlelli,  i  d-tefka  tmurt  n  Leqbayel 
d  asfel  i  ddmen  yimezdaɣ  n  temnaḍin-
nniḍen am Wehran deg 1983, deg Lqesba 
n Lezzayer 1984 d Qsenṭina seg Ctember 
1986. Akka  i  truḥ  am  tquddirt  n  zzit  ɣef 
lkaɣeḍ, yufa-d iman-is udabu yeḥṣel.

«Ass n 19 deg Mayu 1981, nella nessewja-
as-d i yiwen n unejmuɛ ara d-yilin tameddit 
n wass, aten-a-ya kra n yibeɛtiyen iwḍen-d s 
lemɛawna  n  yiɣalen  n  laman,  bdan  kkaten-

Xas  ulamma  terẓa  asalu  n  tugdi, 

tressa  aleqqim  n  usenfali  tebna 
iseɣ  n  uqbayli,  tafsut  Imaziɣen 
tettuneḥsab  d  taɣsert  ideg  i  d-ugmen 
medden asuter n yizerfan addayen n yidles 
d  tmagit  n  yiwen  n  wudem  agejdan  n 
tmurt. Timmuzɣa, iɣef ɛefsen akken ad tt-
snegren imi udem n tmurt-nneɣ jeggren-t 
akken  ad  yaɣ  idles  n  usammer  alemmas, 
idles amaynut ara yerren at tmurt d irbiben 
war  izerfan.  Ɣef  temsalt-a  nqerreb  ɣer 
yiwen  i  iderren  s  liqrib  tamsalt-a, Arezqi 
at  Lɛerbi,  yeqbel  ad  aɣ-d-yerr  ɣef  kra  n 
yisteqsiyen i as-nefka. Walit tiririyin-ines.

35 n yiseggasen ɛeddan, d acut-en 
yiḥulfan-ik ɣef tedyanin n 20 Yebrir 
1980  ?  Ma  yella  wamek,  ad  aɣ-d-
tmeslayeḍ ɣef kra temsal i mazal ur 
d-banent ara ar ass-a ?
Yebrir  80  d  amussu  aɣerfan  meqqren  i 
yekksen  asadel  i  yimaziɣen.  Werɛad  i 
wwḍen  sin  n  yiseggasen  ɣef  tmettant  n 
Boumediene  mi  d-yekker  umussu-ya. 
Yekker  ugdud,  yeddukkel,  iwakken  ad 
d-yini  Dayen!  tfuk  temḥeqrnit.  Uqbel, 
ulac amek ara d-yini umaziɣ awal-is. ayen 
akk icudden ɣer temsalt n tmaziɣt temdel 
fell-as tewwurt. D ayen ara aɣ-yeǧǧen, ad 
nessali deg ccan n umussu n 80 imi agdud 
icqarrew adabu i d-yeffɣen i lbaṭel ɛinani.
Tebda  s  ugdal  n  usarag  i  d-iheyya  Dda 
Lmulud  At  Mɛemmer,  ass  n  10  deg 
Maɣres  1980,  tedda  armi  d  tawaɣit  i 
d-iheyya  udabu  ass  n  20  deg  Yebrir 
1980.  Tamurt  n  Leqbayel  d  tesdawiyin 
n  Lezzayer  tamanaɣt  sɛeddant  ussan  n 
ṭrad  d  ccwal,  meɛna  d  ussan  n  tdukli  d 
usirem n wid yettnaɣen ɣef yizerfan-nsen. 
ɣer  wid  yeddren  ussan-nni,  ad  awen-d-
ini  d  lewqat  iḥersen  iɣef  ara  cfun  alama 
muten. Ma d wid ur teṭṭif ara teswiɛt-nni, 
bɣan  ad  issinen  ugar  ɣef  wayen  yeḍran, 
ad  ten-welheɣ  ad  ɣren  adlis*  i  d-yeffɣen 
aseggas  n  2010  ideg  d-jemɛeɣ  cfawat  n 
yinelmaden  n  tesdawit  n  Tizi-Wezzu  d 
Lezzayer, cfawat n yiselmaden, imsejjayen 
(ṭṭebbat),  imeɣnasen  i  yellan  d  imezwura 
ar  umennuɣ.  Akken  daɣ  ara  afen,  deg 
udlis-a,  ayen  i  d-nnan  ula  d  wid  yellan 
deg lweqt-nni d imdebbren am lwali n Tizi 
Wezzu, anaɣlaf n uselmed aɛlayan akked 
umeqqren n yiɣalen n laman i yekkin deg 

aɣ-d s wayen ufan.»

Nessufuɣ-d  tasɣunt  TAFSUT  s  tufra  deg 
Tizi-Wezzu.  Kra-kra  almi  tuɣal  tettnuzu 
ɛinani.  Nsedda  timsal-nneɣ  akken  iwata 
seg  tazwara n  Maɣres 1981 armi d 19 deg 
Mayyu 1981. D tallit ideg nesɛedda tikti-
nneɣ  i  waṭas  n  medden,  nesedda  idles-
nneɣ,  nefka  i  tugdut  amkan-is  gar-aneɣ 
deg lehna war amennuɣ. 
Ass  n  19  deg  Mayu  1981,  nella 
nessewja-as-d  i  yiwen  n  unejmuɛ  ara 
d-yilin  tameddit  n  wass,  aten-a-ya  kra  n 
yibeɛtiyen iwḍen-d s lemɛawna n yiɣalen 
n laman, bdan kkaten-aɣ-d s wayen ufan. 
D tagnit iwakken ad refden akk iɛeggalen-
nni i iqeddcen ɣef tumast d yidles amaziɣ. 
Nufa-d  iman-nneɣ  deg  22  deg  lḥebs  n 
Lḥerrac. Ḥekmen fell-aɣ deg Tuber 1981. 
amur  ameqqran  fkan-asen  5  n  wayyuren 
kan, uɣalen serḥen-asen, ma d nekkni deg 
4  yid-neɣ  neṭṭef  aseggas  n  lḥebs:  Salaḥ 
Bukrif (ad fell-as yeɛfu yerḥem!), Musṭafa 
Baca, El Qadi lḥsen akked nekk.
  
Tuber  yusa-d  8  n  yiseggasen.  Ur 
tettwaliḍ  ara  belli  tidyanin  n  tmurt 
n  Leqbayel  i  d-yessakin  azzayri  n 
lweqt-nni ?
Ahat  d  ayen  i  d-yeḍran,  meɛna  mebla 
ccek,  tanekkra-nni  i  d-yellan  deg  tmurt 

«Amussu-ya i d-ilulen deg tmurt n Leqbayel, 
yekka-d  Lezzayer,  Bumerdes,  Clef,  Tnes, 
uqbel ad ikemmel tikli, yeɣli-d fell-as udabu 

iwakken ad t-yeḥbes.»

rray i ddmen iwakken ad ḥebsen umussu. 
wigi  merra  llan-d  d  inagan  deg  udlis-a. 
D adlis amezwaru i d-yeffɣen ɣef  Tefsut 
Tamaziɣt,  sarameɣ  ad  ilin  wiyiḍ  ara 
d-yawin ugar n tafat ɣef tallit-a n umezruy.

19  deg  Mayyu  1981,  aseggas  seld 
20  deg  Yebrir,  Tamurt  n  Leqbayel 
tekker-d  daɣen.  Amek  i  tesɛeddam 
tidyanin-a?
Tidyanin n 19 deg Mayyu 1981 i d-yeḍran, 
ladɣa,  deg  la  Soummam  akked  tesdawit 
n  Lezzayer,  kkant-d  seg  leqdic  ameqran 
i  yellan  deg  lawan-nni.  Amedya  seg 
leqdicat-a, ad d-nebder timsirin n tmaziɣt 
i  d-tessuddus  tdukla  tadelsant  n  tesdawit 
n  Lezzayer.  D  timsirin  i  d-yettak  Mass 
Salem  Caker.  Mačči  kan  d  leqqraya, 
meɛna  d  tagnit  n  uskasi  ɣef  temsalt  n 
tumast,  d  yidles  amaziɣ.  Deg  lawan-nni, 

n  Leqbayel,  ɣas  akken  yella-d  wayen  i 
d-yellan  seg  tama  n  udabu,  thud  lḥiḍ-nni 
n tsusmi, tcerreg abrid yettawin ar tlelli s 
wudem-is wessiɛen. Seld tidyanin n 1981 
deg Bgayet akked Lezzayer, amussu yuɣal 
cwiya ar deffir meɛna ur yemmut ara. Seg 
1983 yuɣal-d uḥerrek, ladɣa win i d-wwin 
tarwa  n  yimeɣrasen  i  d-yerran  ar  wallaɣ 
ayen  i  nessutur  deg  Yebrir  1980  deg 
wayen  yerzan  idles  d  tugdudt.  Annect-a 
ɣer tama n usuter-nsen agejdan i yekkaten 
ɣef terwiḥin n yimawlan-nsen i yemmuten 
ɣef Lezzayer n tlelli. 
Amussu-ya 
tmurt  n 
i  d-ilulen  deg 
Leqbayel,  yekka-d  Lezzayer,  Bumerdes, 
Clef, Tnes, uqbel ad ikemmel tikli, yeɣli-d 
fell-as  udabu  iwakken  ad  t-yeḥbes.  Syin 
akkin,  isexdem  ideqqacen-is  iwakken  ad 
as-ɛiwden  ljerya  i  umussu-ya,  ad  ikcem 
ɣer uxxam ṭmana!

D annect-a akk i d-iheggan abrid i tedyanin 
n  Tuber  1988.  Adabu  yufa-d  iman-is 
yewḥel,  imi  tixnanasin-nni-ines  kksent 
fell-as sser gar tmura n lberra.

Seg 1980 ar ass-a, amek i tettwaliḍ 
amecwar i d-tewwi tumast d tutlayt 
n tamaziɣt? 
Ur  ilaq  ara  ad  nettu,  deg  yiseggasen  70, 
win yebɣan ad ikcem ar lḥebs ad yeddem 
deg  ufus-is  tira  n  tifinaɣ!  Tidayin  n  80 
wwint-d  tilelli  i  Umaziɣ,  udem  amaziɣ  n 
tmurt n yuɣal ikcem ɣer wallaɣ n udabu, 
yesteɛref  yi-s  belli  d  aḥric  n  tumast  n 
tamaziɣt 
Lezzayer.  Seg  2002 
tekcem  ɣer  tmendawt  d  tutlayt  taɣelnawt 
daɣen.  Meɛna  agur  mazal  ur  yekkis  ara. 
Tamaziɣt  mazal  ur  tufi  ara  iman-is. Ama 
deg uɣerbaz, ama deg tɣamsa neɣ ula deg 
ttawilat  n  taywalt  ladɣa  tiliẓri.  skecmen 
tamaziɣt  deg  teḥnact-nni  n  le  folklorisme 
d wayen ur nemɛin. Ma tella cciɛa i ttaken 
medden  i  yir  leqdic,  TV4  ad  tawi  cciɛa 
ɛlayen  ilmend  n  wayen  i  txeddem  mgal 
tamaziɣt.

tutlayt 

Mazal  adabu  azzayri  yettara  iman-
is ur yettwali ur yessal, am wakken 
mačči  d  lawan  iwakken  ad  tekcem 
tumast  tamaziɣt  ɣer  tmedawt  s 
wudem unsid. Acu i d rray-ik?
Adabu  ur  iɛuẓey,  ur  iderɣel.  Yettwalqem 
s  txellalt  n  tiɛurrebt-tineslemt  yettagaden 
seg  tmaziɣt  d  wayen  akk  icudden  ɣer-s. 
Adabu izmer ad d-yuɣal alama d tixnasin-
is  ideg  yuɣ  tanummi.  Seg Tuber  1988  ar 
ass-a,  nutni  kkaten  amek  ara  d-ajjwen 
lmut  i  tmaziɣt.  Sɛan  lweqt,  sɛan  ttawilat 
i  waya.  Dayen  i  nettwali,  adabu  isekcem 
iqeddacen-is ula gar yimeɣnasen iwakken 
ad naɣen gar-asen, ad msebḍun.  
Mebla  ccek,  asekcem  n  tmaziɣt  deg 
tmendawt i d-iteddun yesɛa azal-is, meɛna 
ur nwiɣ ara ad yili d ddwa ilaqan i umuḍin. 
Acu  kan,  ala  leqdic  zeddigen  akked 
uxemmem  ɣef  wamek  ara  yili  umennuɣ 
ɣef  yimal  n  tmaziɣt  ara  d-yawin  ugar  n 
waya. D ayen i ugdeɣ nesruḥuy seg-s aḥric 
akka nella tura.  

M. A.

deg umayyur Tiɣremt

Tazɣent n Tmaziɣt Deg ukabar PPA-MTLD 1949

Amezruy. Gar yinelmaden-a, ad naf Ɛemmar Uld Ḥemmuda win yettwaḥsaben d tigejdit gar wid 
yessawalen s yisem n tmaziɣt daxel n CA n MTLD ɣer yidis n Weɛli Bennay ; yeɛdem ṭrad Uld 
Ḥemmuda aseggas n 1956 imi cellen-as-d yiwet n ttuhma “Tamaziɣt d temṣalit d tcuyuɛit”.  Akka 
i  t-id-yura  Rabeḥ  Lewnis  deg  udlis-is  i  d-yeffɣen  deg  usegga  2002,  yenna  :  «  Ur  yezmir  ara 
amagnay, ad yegzem awal ma yella d aheyyi n yimhersen neɣ d timlilit kan akka n wazal n tlatin 
n  yinelmaden iqbayliyen deg yiwet n tesnawit deg tmanaɣt n Lezzayer, daɣen ɣur amḍan-a 
anager kraḍ n yinelmaden i d-yusan seg temnaḍin-nniḍen, yiwen seg Clef, wayeḍ seg Xmis 
Melyana, ma d wis kraḍ yettbin-d d amzabi seg temnaḍt n ɣerdaya, ihi tameslayt-is d yiwet n 
tanatala, tekcem deg tmaziɣt. »

tuget-agi

yebɣi wara ad teqqel ad tselḥu s 
ukabar  acuyuɛi  afransawi  itri  n 
tefriqt ugafa, aken i yella Lɛimac 
Ɛli  deffir  ubeddel  n  ubrid  n 
tmeslemt  daxel  n  ukabar  imi  i 
ittekka  akked  Msali  Lḥaǧ  deg

temlilit-nnsen  akked  «  Cakib

d-yekcem talemmast, iwakken ur 
d-yettili wara miḥyaf gar waɛrab 
akked Umaziɣ.
Yeḍra-d  kra  n  umennuɣ  gar  sin 
yixfawen  iqbayliyin  i  ikfan  s

yezdi,  yebɣa  akk  ad  itteki  deg 
uslelli n tmurt », yerna-d daɣen : 
«  cukkeɣ lezzayer ur tezmir ara 
ad tilli d taɛrabt naɣ d Tamaziɣt ; 
wamma nettat d tazzayrit… tezdi 
ur  tbeṭṭu  ara  ».  Ccil,  ɣas  akken 
yeskaddeb  s  wayen  i  yesɛa  d 
tinniga  maca  aṭas 
i  mazal

‹‹Tira akken i teshel i tuɛer !››

Tira. Tasekla taqbaylit mazal tettarew-d imura. Yal aseggas ttlalen-d deg waṭas yid-sen am yiferraǧ n 
tsekkurt yesmirǧiḥen di tɣaltin. Deg wass n 30 duǧember 1989, tlul-d teqcict yeṭṭfen imru ass-a akken 
ad taru s teqbaylit n lejdud-ines. Di taddart n KUKU, taɣiwant n At Yeḥya tlul-d Cabḥa Ben GANA, am 
yimɣi d-ilulen di tmazirt n yijeǧǧigen. Teɣra di tesnawit n teqcicin n Micli anda d-tewwi akayad n l’BAK, 
tekcem ɣer tesdawit n Mulud At-Mɛemmer n Tizi-Uzzu anda d-tewwi turagt di tutlayt n tmaziɣt deg 
useggas n 2012. Cabḥa ur teḥbis ara kan deg uswir-nni, tkemmel l’Mastir di tesnilest deg useggas n 
2017 ɣer da. 

Rnu  ɣer-s  ttwaliɣ  udem  n  tira-
tmuɣliwin  yi-d-ttaken 
inu  di 
yimeɣriyen.»

D acu ibeddlen deg-m deg 
wasmi teggiḍ timliliyin-agi i 
mi temlaleḍ d imeɣriyen udem 
ar wudem ? 

«Timliliyin-a 

ttaǧǧant-iyi  ad 

sekcebreɣ  ugar  di  tira,  fkant-
iyi-d  daɣen  tabɣest  akken  ad 
fkeɣ  ugar,  imi  tura  mačči  kan  i 
yiman-iw i ttaruɣ, llan imeɣriyen 
ar tama-w.»
Ahat tebɣiḍ ad d-ternuḍ awal 
uqbel ad nessali adiwani-a?
«Ddeqs  n  wungalen  i  d-yefɣen 
ayen 
ladɣa

d 

yessefraḥen! A win yufan kan ad 
ilin  daɣen  wid  ara  d-asen-
yuɣalen  s  lmendad  s  usenqed 
usnan.»

Tanemmirt-inem, afud 
igerzen deg umecwar-inem.

«Tanemmirt-ik.»

Aḥric 7 wis ssa
Llsan  akk  ticluḥin,  sburren  akk 
iqelmunen,  yal  wa  yewwi  yid-s 
taftilt deg ufus-is. Ageffur mazal 
yekkat, sya ɣer da ad d-remmeg 
tegnawt,  ad  d-breqq.  Ageffur 
igellu-d s ixeclawen n udfel. 
Lɣaci  bḍan  d 
tirebbuɛa,  yal 
tarbaɛt  tewwi  tama,  ta  terra  ar 
usammar,  ta  ar  umalu,  ta  ur 
ugafa.  Alarmi  aṭas  yiwet  n 
tarbaɛt, 
tufa  aɣyul  yeɣli  ar 
seddaw  ubrid  s  ttɛebga-ines,  ur 
yemmut  ara,  maca  yejreḥ  mliḥ. 
Kra  isurifen  akken,  s  ufella  n 
ubrid, ufan Uqasi yeɣli di tbaɛruṛt 
n yidammen, tagelzimt tenta gar 
tuyat-is. Tafekka-s telxes, teqqur. 
Fsin-as  ttɛebga  i  waɣyul-nni, 
neḥrent s axxam.

Tiɣremt  -  Un 42   Arim 20 yebrir 2020

Tadiwennit d unaẓur acennay ATMANI
« Tafsut n yimaziɣen d azamul n umennuɣ d tnegmit »
Asmekti. S yisem-is n tidet, ilul-d Ait Atmane M’hemmed, neɣ Ḥemmic At Wadda, nennum nessawal-
as Dda Ḥemmic, ass n 11 deg ctember 1945 deg taddart  Zaknun, lɛerc At Buɛekkac, taɣiwant At 
Wasif deg udrar ɛlayen.

ATMANI, 

Dda 
neɣ 
Ḥemmic  akken 
i  as-
sawalen  yimeddukkal-is 
d  leḥbab-is,  d  amdan  iḥemmlen 
adrar, d mmi-s n ǧerǧer ɛlayen, d 
adrar i d aɣbalu yis. Deg useggas-
nni  1968,  i  yessekles  aḍebsi-is 
amezwaru  (33  tours),  win  id 
t-yewwin deg ubrid n tẓuri, abrid 
n tmussni.
Abrid  n  tẓuri  d  win  i  ikemmel 
netta d kra n yimeddukkal-is am 
Ben 
Muḥemmed 
Ḥanafi, 
Ben  Muhub 
Muḥemmed 
yettwasnen  s  yisem  Muḥuc, 
Buɛlam Awaḍi, d umeddakkel-is 
acqiq,  win  ukkud  ur  iferreq, 
acennay  Ayet  Bumehdi,  akked 
kra n wiyaḍ.
Aseggas n 80 d win ur nezmir ad 
iɛeddi  kan  akka,  d  win 
id 
d-yeǧǧan later-is deg leqbayel, d 
win  i  yellan  d  sebba  n  uḥerrek 
deg  Lezzayer.  Tafsut  n  80 
teǧǧa-d  later  ula  deg  unaẓur 
ATMANI.  S  ubrid  n 
tẓuri, 
Atmani  yemmeslay-d,  yenna-d 
ayen iwala d tmuɣli-is ɣef tefsut 
n 
yecna, 
yessekles  takalast  (album)  «ay 
arraw imaziɣen» i d-yeffɣen deg 
useggas 1981.
Deg  useggas  1985,  Atmani 
yessekcem sin warraw-is Lexḍer 
d  Nurdin  iwumi  qqaren  Kudy, 
yesɛan 14 d 13 n yiseggasen, ɣer 
ccna  deg  tkalast  «A  Tamurt  n 
yimaziɣen» ; d takalast mucaɛen 
aṭas.
Dda Ḥemmic neɣ Atmani yeqbel 
ad  d-yerr  ɣef  kra  n  yisteqsiyen 
ilmend n usmekti wis 40 n tefsut 
n yimaziɣen, s ttawil n tilifun.

tmanyin, 

yenna, 

Tiɣremt : Azul a Dda Ḥemmic, 
tettidireḍ  akman-agi 
Amek 
kečč mmi-s n udrar deg tmurt 
n Fransa ?
Atmani  :  D  tazɣent  tadawsant 
urǧin tɛedda ; d tin iwumi neqqar 
s  teqbaylit-nneɣ  lgirra  mebla 
akerṭuc. Ur yeshil ara ad qqimeɣ 
acḥal  mebla  ma  walaɣ,  ma  ẓriɣ 
ma, qesreɣ d warraw-iw, iḥbiben-
iyi-
iḥemmleɣ 
iw,  wid 
iḥemmlen,  ur  yeshil  ara  ;  maca 
aḥezzeb  yerra  leqḍeɛ,  ttif  xir 
amdan  ad  yekmen  kan  deg 
uxxam-is.  Seg  wass  ɣer  wass 
nettaɣ  tannumi,  akken  ad  neṭṭef 
deg 
tdawsa-nneɣ, 
teffɣeɣ  leḥḥuɣ  akka  cwiṭ,  aya 
yettili-d s lemḥadra d uḥezzeb.

tezmert  d 

id 

I lukan deg wat wasif i telliḍ 
ussan-a n lekmin, amek ara 
tidireḍ lekmin-a ?
Akken  xeddmeɣ  dag-i  deg 
Fransa  ara  xedmeɣ  deg  wat 
wasif,  ad  qqimeɣ  deg  uxxam, 
ulac i yecban tiɣimit deg uxxam-
ik deg tallit yecban tag-i. Ayen i 
d  iyi-sferḥen  aṭas  mi  ara  twaliḍ 
ad tesleḍ amek i suddsent iman-
nsent tuddar n leqbayel akken ad 
qablent  aṭṭan-agi. 
Iɣermanen, 
neɣ 
imezdaɣ  dduqsen  mliḥ, 
tili 
bedden  mliḥ  akken  ad 
lemḥarba ɣef watmaten-nsen, ɣef 
taddart  s  umata,  akken  ad 
sbeɛden anṭaḍ. Ma twaliḍ neɣ ad 

tesleḍ  s  wakaten  neɣ  leryuy  i 
refden 
imezdaɣ  ɣef  wayen 
yerzan  asizdeg  d  tdawsa,  ad 
tferḥeḍ kan s tuddsa n leqbayel d 
tuddar  akken  ad  yili  uḥareb  d 
usemnaɛ  n  yidartiwen  s  umata. 
Yewwi-d  ɣef  tmurt  n  leqbayel 
akken ad tkemmel deg ubrid-a n 
uḥareb  s  uqader  n  yiwellihen 
idawsanen.

D acu-ten waktayen-ik ɣef 20 
seg yebrir ?
D  azemz  i  d  iyi-d-yesmektayen 
tizzeɣzeɣt n udabu i d-yeɣlin ɣef 
tesdawit 
n  Tizi-wezzu.  D 
aḥerrem  n  tlelli-nneɣ  d  tuṭṭfa-
nneɣ  deg  yidles  d 
tutlayt 
tamaziɣt.  Cfiɣ  mliḥ,  azekka-nni 
ṣubbeɣ  ɣer  Tizi,  ɛeddaɣ  sdat 
tesdawit  Medduḥa, 
tiɣremt  n 
hedreɣ 
yinalmaden. 
Yesseqlaleḥ-iyi lbaṭel-nni yeḍran 
ussan-nni.  Ayen  ixedmen  deg 
yinalmaden  ass-nni,  yerwi-iyi 
akk,  uɣaleɣ  xedmeɣ  tazlit-nni 
«Ay  Arraw  n  Yimaziɣen,  a  wid 
Ɣlayen, A tarwa n Udrar n nnif». 
D  tazlit  neɣ  d  tasfift  i  d-yeffɣen 
deg useggas 1981.

akked 

D acu i tzemreḍ ad aɣ-t-id-
tiniḍ ɣef tefsut n yimaziɣen ?
Tafsut  n  yimaziɣen  d  azamul  n 
unamer  d  umennuɣ  d  tnegmit  d 
usuter ; xas tamsalt-a n tmagit, d 
tamsalt  taqburt,  d  tin  yebdan 
acḥal  d  aseggas  uqbel  1980.  Ad 
rreɣ  tajmilt  i  kra  n  wid  d  tid 
yennuɣen  ɣef  yidles  d  tutlayt  d 
tnaṣlit neɣ tamagit-nneɣ. Ur ilaq 
ara  ad  nettu  tiɣtas  (victimes)  n 
tefsut  taberkant  akked  twaculin-
nsen.  Ar  ass-a  mazal  wid 
yettnaɣen,  xeddmen  akken  ad 
rren  azal  ad  d-sbegnen  tigemmi 
tanaṣlit, tajaddit-nneɣ.

igzem-aɣ 

39 n yiseggasen nesmektay-d 
akk tafsut n yimaziɣen, 
asseggas-a wis 40 ur yettili ara 
usmekti s sebba n unfafad-aa 
n coronavirus d ukman-a i 
nettwakmen, d acu-tt tmuɣli-
ik ɣef usmekti wis 40 ur nettili 
ara ?
S  tidet  d  tallit  iweɛren  mliḥ, 
aṭṭan-agi 
kulci, 
iḥerrem-aɣ  deg  kulci,  timlilit, 
timeɣriwin,  ula  d 
asmekti, 
lǧanaza  iḥerrem-aɣ  seg-s,  aya 
ilmend  n  uḥareb  ɣef  terwḥin-
nneɣ akk. Maca alɣagduden (les 
masses  media),  am  tilibizyuwat, 
iɣmisen,  radyuwat  n 
tmaziɣt 
aladɣa, yewwi-d fell-asen akk ad 
d-mmeslayen 
ad 
d-smektin  akk  ɣef 
tefsut  n 
yimaziɣen akked tefsut taberkant. 
D lwaǧeb ad d-nsemekti i tsuta-a 
d  yilmeẓyen  akk  ur  nessin,  ur 
neḥḍir i tefsut n tmanyin, acḥal d 
i 
argaz  d 
yenneɛtaben,  i  yefkan  tudert-
nsen,  akken  idles  d  tutlayt-nneɣ 
ad 
ten-iseffeḍ  ara 
idiren,  ur 
ucengu n tmaziɣt.

i  yeɣlin, 

ussan-a, 

tmeṭṭut 

D acu-t umur i d-yefka unaẓur 
i yidles d tutlayt tamaziɣt ?
Anaẓur  d  amaru,  d  amekla,  d 

aselmad, d anelmad, d acennay d 
kra  akk  n  win  iqeddcen  ɣef 
unegmu  d  uǧuǧǧeg  n  tutlayt  d 
yidles n tmaziɣt. Anaẓur d netta i 
d-yessakayen tinuggiyin ; aladɣa 
tazlit  neɣ  acennay  d  amrig,  d 
allal  iwatan  i  useddu  n  yizen 
amaziɣ, izen n usaki d umennuɣ, 
izen n takti.

D  acu-tt  tmuɣli-ik  ɣef  yimal  n 
tmurt  n  lezzayer  d  yimal  n 
tmaziɣt ?
Tamurt teḥwaǧ irgazen d tlawin i 
d-yekkan  seg  tmetti  taɣarimt  d 
wid  yeɣran.  Imdanen  zeddigen, 
wid  yeṣfan  akken  ad  beddlen 
tamurt  s  telqayt.  Ɣef  tmaziɣt, 
aṭas  i  tuẓ,  maca  mazal  aṭas  n 
yixeddim. Aselmed-is ilaq ad yili 
d  anzuccal  (obligatoire)  mačči  s 
ttriḥ  neɣ  s  usuter  n  yimawlan  n 
ad 
unelmad.  D 
lwaǧeb 
yettuselmed 
umezruy-nneɣ 
aḥeqqi,  amezruy  n  yilaw,  mačči 
win n lekdeb, amezruy n tmazɣa 
asertan,  imetti,  adamsan  win  n 
tallit n Gaya, Syfaks d Masnsen. 
Ad  yettuselmed  deg  uɣerbaz 
azzayri umezruy n yimenza-nneɣ 
«Imaziɣen».

D acu tzemreḍ ad t-id-tiniḍ ɣef 
uselway-agi d unabaḍ-is 
ugziren ?
Ɣef tuttra-agi ma tessurfeḍ-iyi ad 
d-rreɣ s yiwet n tenfalit n umaru 
Afransis  Chateaubriand  anda  i 
as-yenna : «yella uṣaḍuf n tudeba 
tameẓẓult 
timetti, 
yeslugunen 
tameẓẓult 
i  yernan 
tamatut 
tawḥidt.  Aṣaḍuf-a  ameqran  d 
tmeẓẓult-a  tameqrant  d  izugla  n 
yizerfan  igmawiyen  n  umdan  i 
slugunen iteffaren ; acku d ateffar 
id  d-yeslalayen  azref,  mačči  d 
azref  id-yeslalayen  ateffar».  («Il 
y  a  une  loi  morale  qui  règle  la 
société,  une  légitimité  générale 
légitimité 
qui 
particulière.  Cette  grande  loi  et 
cette  grande  légitimité  sont  la 
jouissance des droits naturels de 
l’homme, réglés par les devoirs ; 
car  c’est  le  devoir  qui  crée  le 
droit,  et  non  le  droit  qui  crée  le 
devoir  »).  Ma  d  nekk  aql-i  d 
ugdud.

domine 

la 

Ma nuɣal-d ɣer tezlit, tḥebseḍ 
ccna neɣ yella kra i tettheyyiḍ 
?
Ccna ḥebseɣ-t deg useggas 1999. 
S yin d afella xedmeɣ ɣef yiwen 
n  usentel  i  yewwin  mliḥ  ul-iw 
«tamagit  taqbaylit»,  ɣef  waya 
skelseɣ  snat 
tezlatin  yewwin 
azwel  «Ay  Aqbayli  Mebla 
nekkwa»  i  d-yeffɣen  di  yebrir 
2017.
Imal  d  ayla  n  tsuta-a  tilemẓit 
iwumi  ssarameɣ  afud  igerrzen 
wa  ssarmeɣ  ad  teg  iseɣ  i  tezlit 
taqbaylit.

Awal-ik n taggara !

tamezwarut deg useggas 1958 mi

Burusu  messuseḍ,  Tusa-yi-d

Arumi.  Yella  deg

akked  Si  Ḥmimi.  Membaɛed 
timunent  yekki  deg  waṭas  n 
leqdicat  idelsanen  am  wakken 
iɛwen 
yinaẓuren 
imeẓẓyanen  iwakken  ad  refden 
tizlit  taqbaylit  s  yiseɣ.  Mohand 
Arezki  Bouzid  ilul  deg  tmurt  n 
taddart  El  Qelɛa

i 
adewwar Leqser, aɣir n Bgayet.
S  yisem  n  yineɣmasen  Tiɣremrt 
nessaram  ssber  i  twacult-is,  d 
talwit i yiẓiɣer n lmerḥum.

TADAWSA

Tiɣremt  -  Un 42   Arim 20 yebrir 2020

15
Kra n talɣut ɣef unfafad Covid-19
i d-tefka Tuddsa Tamaḍalt n Tezmert

ad t-yenṭeḍ waṭṭan ma yeqreb zdat win 
yuḍnen yusu-d yefka-d timiqwa, netta 
yerra nnefs yeqreb-it ddaw lmitra.

-Ur  tettut  isalen  i  d-yettawḍen  akken 
ad tawim lexbar anda yewweḍ waṭṭan 
COVID-19.  Ma  tzemrem  ur  ttsafaret, 
xususen ma meqqer laɛmer-nwen neɣ 
tuḍneɣ aṭṭan n sskeṛ, wul d yedmarren.
Acuɣer? Acku deg temnaḍin-a, aṭṭan 
yeshel ad k-yenṭeḍ.

anda  tetteddu  liḥala.  Ihi  nadit  ɣef 
yisalan.
Tzemrem ad tmenɛem, ma : Tessiridem 
ifassen-nwen,  s  hydroalcool  neɣ  s 
sabun d waman.
Acuɣer  ?  Asired  s  hydroalcool  neɣ 
sabun  d  waman  yettnuɣ  anfafad  ma 
yella deg yifassen.-
-Ad yibɛid yiwen ɣef medden yettusun 
neɣ  iɛeṭsen,  ma  ulac  akk,  s  wazal  n 
lmitra.
Acuɣer  ?  M’ara  yeɛṭes  yiwen  neɣ 
yusu,  iḍeggir-d  timiqwa  izemren  ad 
glunt  s  unfafad.  Ma  tqerbeḍ,  tzemreḍ 
ad t-tesnufseḍ. 
-Ur  ttnalet  allen-nwen,  tinzer  d  yimi-
nwen.

Acu-t coronavirus ?
D 
tarbaɛt  meqqren  n  yinfafaden 
izemren ad snetḍen lehlak i umdan neɣ 
i uɣersiw. Neẓra, ɣef wayen imalen ar 
umdan,  aṭas  n  coronavirus  i  yellan,  d 
wid izemren ad ǧǧen tuḍna ad taɣ deg 
usnufes,  s  usḥerḥer  alamma  d  wayen 
yugaren aya, am tiwḍi ar lehlak (Mers) 
neɣ (SRAS).

Acu-t COVID-19 ?
COVID-19, d isem n tuḍna tamsalmit 
i  d-yettasen  seg  unfafad  coronavirus 
i  d-ibanen.  Anfafad-a  d  tuḍna-ya  ur 
ttwassnen ara yakanqbel ad yucaɛ deg 
Wuhan (Ccin) deg waggur n dujenber 
2019.

Amek  ara  yeɛqel  yiwen  yuḍen 
COVID-19 ?
Leɛlamat sway ara d-yawi lexbar yiwen 
belli  yuḍen  COVID-19,  tbeddu-d  s 
tawla,  facal  d  tusut  yekkawen.  Llan 
imuḍan iɣef d-irennu lqerḥ, idammen 
deg  tinzar,  ad  d-yetteɣlay  uxenziz, 
lqerḥ  n  taɣect  d  tazzla  n  tɛebbuṭ. 
Leɛlamat-a  mezziyit,  ulac  ara  yagad 
yiwen. Ggran-d imuḍan n waṭṭanen ur 
nḥellu (aṭṭan wul, n ssker). Ma tebda-
ten-d  tawla,  tusut  d  luɛara  n  tririn  n 
nnefs, ilaq ad walin ṭbib.  

Anfafad n waṭṭan COVID-19, wis 
ma  yezmer  ad  yenṭeḍ  yiwen  s 
lhawae ?
Tizrawin  i  d-yellan  ar  wass-a  d  tid  i 
d-yeqqaren  belli  anfafad  COVID-19 
ineṭṭeḍ  s  tzmlilit  d  tmiqwa  i  d-yerra 
yiwen s nnefs, mačči s lhawa.

Yezmer ad ɣ-isehlek win ur nesɛi 
leɛlamat n waṭṭan COVID-19 ?
Aṭṭan  ineṭṭeḍ  s  tmiqwa  ara  d-yefk 
yiwen  seg  yimi  neɣ  seg  tanzarin 
ma  yusu.  Ulac  lxuf  deg  win  ur  nesɛi 
leɛlamat,  neɣ  ad  d-nini  qlilit.  Ihi  win 
ittusun cwiṭ yif ma yebɛed yiwen fell-
as.

Zemreɣ ad aḍneɣ COVID-19, ma 
nnuleɣ ixxan n win yuḍnen ?
Tuḍna n COVID-19 s temlilit neɣ ma 
yennul  yiwen  ixxan  n  win  yuḍnen,  d 
ayen  izemren  ad  d-yili,  maɛna  qlilit. 
Anfafad  yezmer  ad  yili  deg  yixxan, 
maɛna werjin yucaɛ s ubrid-a. acu kan, 
ur  ilaq  ɣef  yiwen  ad  yettu  ad  isizdeɣ 
ifassen-is,  mi  d-yeffeɣ  seg  cicma  neɣ 
qbel ad yečč.

Amek i yettenṭaḍ COVID-19 ?
Aṭṭan COVID-19 isenṭaḍ-it win yeṭṭef 
unfafad.  Aṭṭan  neṭṭeḍ  s  tmiqwa  i 
d-iteffɣen seg yimi neɣ seg tanzarin n 
win  yuḍnen  m’ara  d-yusu.  Timiqwa-
ya,  zemrent  ad  rsent  ɣef  leqcuc  neɣ 
ɣef wayen i d-yezzin i umdan-a. Aṭṭan 
ibeddu-d  ma  nennul  leqcuc-a  neɣ 
nennul  amḍiq  anda  yenṭeḍ  unfafad, 
syin ad nekmez allen-nneɣ neɣ tinzert 
neɣ imi. Akken daɣen i yezmer yiwen 

Amek  zemreɣ  ad  ḥadreɣ  iman-
iw,  ad  ḥedreɣ  ɣef  wid  i  yi-d-
iqerben ?
I medden d tirni.
Ilaq  ad  tnadim  ɣef  lexbar  anda  wḍen 
ɣef  waṭṭan  anda  yewweḍ  neɣ  ɣef 
unfafad, aya ad t-tafem deg site OMS 
yakk d tneɣlasin n tezmert n tal tamurt. 
Aṭas  n  tmura  menɛent,  ma  neddem 
taluft  n  Ccinwa,  anda  aṭṭan  sneqsen 
deg uzuzer-ines. Maca yiwen ur yeẓri 

Ayen 
ilaq  ad  yexdem  yiwen 
yejban  ar  temnaḍin  anda  aṭṭan 
COVID-19  yucaɛ,  deg  rbeɛtac 
ussan-aya.
-Walit acu ilaqen ad yexdem yiwen i 
lemḥdra.
-Ma  tebdam  tettḥulfam  s  lihala  n 
tezmert-nwen  tenbeddal,  ɣas  ulamma 
cwiṭ (ttecqiqa, tawla telḥeq ar 37,3 °C d 
tanzarin ttazzalent), qimet deg uxxam 
alamma teḥlim. Ma ulac amsaɛef, ara 
yettkelfen  yes-wen,  fɣeɣ  s  tekmamt 
akken dɣa ur tessedraɛem i ḥeḍ.
Acuɣer?  Ur  ttemyagaret  d  lɣir,  ur 
ttruḥut  ar  sbitarat,  akken  ad  tent-
teǧǧem  ad  xedmen  axeddim-nsen 
akken ilaq, ad mendeden fell-awen ɣef 
waṭṭan COVID-19 d waṭṭanen niḍen.
-Ma  tebda-kun  tawla,  tusut  d  diqan, 
siwlet  i  ṭbib  s  lɛejlan,  tinim-as  ma 
tsafrem ar wanda n kra.
Acuɣer?  Ma  tessawlem-as,  ad  kun-
yenced s lemɣawla anda ilaq ad terrem. 
Akken  ula  d  kunwi  ad  tmenɛem  deg 
waṭṭan  COVID-19,  ur  tessehlakem 
wiyiḍ. 
Tuddsa  Tamaḍalt  n  Tezmert,  teṭṭafar 
isalenseg  wass  ɣer  wass  ɣef  waṭṭan 
COVID-19. 
Walit site-ines :
https://www.who.int/emergencies/
diseases/novel-coronavirus-2019/
situation-reports/. 

Tasuqelt sɣur :
Mohand Ait Ighil

Acuɣer ? Ifassen d wid idelwiḥen ɣef 
waṭas leqcuc, yezmer ad awin anfafad. 
Ma  yekcem  seg  unfafad  seg  wallen 
neɣ tinzert neɣ imi, ad taḍnem.
-Ilaq  ad  tqadrem  lqanun  n  tezdeg  n 
usnufes akken dɣa wid i wen-d-yezzin 
ilaq  ad  xedmen  am  kunwi.  Ilaq  ad 
yusu  neɣ  yeɛṭes  yiwen  ar  zdaxel  n 
tiɣmert-is, neɣ ar tmucwar ara iḍegger 
imar-imar.
Acuɣer?  Timiqwa 
i  d-iteffɣen 
s  usnufes  zuzurent  anfafad.  Ma 
tezdeg,  ad 
ilugan-a  n 
ttwaqadren 
tselkem imdanen i wen-d-yezzin.
-Ma  tḥulfam  s  lehlak,  qimet  deg 
uxxam.  Ma  tzad  tawla  neɣ  tusut  neɣ 
luɛara deg tririn n nnefs, siwlet i ṭbib, 
qbal ma teffɣem, ḍefrem ayen ara wen-
id-yini. Ur tettuɣ dɣa isalen n tezmert 
n tmurt anda tellim.
Acuɣer?  Acku  d  nutni  i  izemren 
ad  wen-id-yefk 
imaynuten, 
iseḥḥan  ɣef  temnaḍin  anda  tellim. 
Akken daɣen, anagar ṭbib i izemren ad 
wen-id-yini anwa sbitar i wen-ilaqen.

TAFSUT N 80

Tiɣremt  -  Un 42   Arim 20 yebrir 2020

Tamuɣli d tnagit ɣef 20 yebrir 1980
Tafsut. Ass n 20 yebrir 1980 d ass anda kecmen yimsulta (iɣallen n laman) ɣer tesdawit n Tizi wezzu, 
lewzin n Sonelec, Sbitar n Tizi wezzu d kra n yigrawen yersen deg lewzin n uceṭṭiḍ n Draɛ Benxedda. 
Iseggasen  i  d-iḍefren  20  yebrir  nebɣa  ad  t-nerr  d  ass  aɣelnaw  mgal  lbaṭel  d  temḥeqranit  acku  d 
annect-a  i  d-yellan  ass-nni.  Dɣa  asfugel  n  20  yebrir  yeslul-d  timesbaniyin  tidelsanin  i  wakken  ad 
d-neffeɣ seg usentel n temḥeqranit.

TAFSUT N 80

19

Tafsut n Yimaziɣen, lemmr mačči d Nutni
Amezruy. Ah taddart-iw, nennejla mebla ma neẓra sani la nteddu, ladɣa ma telliḍ d aqcic, d acawrar 
neɣ d ilemẓi, aṭas n yimdanen ara d-temlileḍ deg tudert-ik akken kan ara k-yefk umnar n tewwurt, 
wanag ma tɛeddaḍ akkin i tlisa n tddart-ik, lɛarc-ik neɣ taaɣiwant ideg tettidireḍ, aṭas ara n yiwudam 
ara d-temmlileḍ. Akka i tella ddunit qqaren ddu ɣef tmura ad tissineḍ, ɣar ad tfehmeḍ, ddu d yirgazen 
ad tessineḍ.

Seg  wasmi  tebna  yemma-as 

n  ddunit,  amdan  yezga  d 
anadi ɣef uɣrum-is, d anadi 
ɣef tlelli-s, acukan teddun waman 
akken  bɣan  mačči  akken  nebɣa. 
awal-nni  qqaren  yimezwura-
nneɣ: “ffeɣ ad tessineḍ”, ẓay deg 
unamak,  ladɣa  ma  d-temlileḍ 
imdanen  ijerben,  wid  yeɣran, 
wid  yeẓran  sani  teddunt  temsal. 
Mi ara telliḍ d acawrar nadi fell-
asen,  acku  ɣas  tekkreḍ-d  ulac 
idlisen  deg  uxxam  d  wigi  ara 
k-yellin d allen, aṭas n yilmeẓyen 
akka  am  nekkni  neɣ  cuban  ɣur-
neɣ,  lemmer  mačči  d  tadukkli  d 
temlilit  yid-sen ahat tudert ad tili 
d abrid nniḍen.
Seg  taddart  ɣer  tesdawit,  anta 
tasdawit, ulac-itt akk deg tedmi-k 
ay  amdan,  maca  mi  ara  d-tawiḍ 
tasarut-nni n leqraya iɣef ttweṣṣin 
yimawla-nneɣ,  ad  yeffeɣ  leɛtab 
ɣer  tafat,  tasarut  d  lbak,  aḥric-
nniḍen di tudert, seg tesnawit ɣer 
tesdawit. Tasdawit, d tallit ladɣa 
inekkni  i  d-yufan  iman-nneɣ  dg 
tesdawit  n  Wahran,  aṭas  i  iɣilen 
ualc i yellan deg-s, ih d tasdawit i 
d-yefkan  aṭas  n  yimussnawen 
tmetti, 
ama  deg 
tussnamadan, 
tutlayin 
tiberraniyin,  d  wataṣ  n  yiḥricen 
nniḍen. 
Deg  yiseggasen-nni  n  temrawt 
taberkant, 
tesdawit  n 
Wahran tbedd, tugi ayen i iḍerrun 
deg tmurt deg tallit-nni taqesḥant 
i  ihuz  rrebrab,  maca  xas  ṭṭuqten 
yimselmaẓriyen,  tikkwal  ad  as-
teqqraeḍ  ḥala  nutni  i  yeṭṭfen 
annar  n  tesertit,  maca  igenni 
yeččur  d  itran,  wid  ɣef  ḍallent 
wallen-k  banen,  maca  wiyyaḍ 

tussna  n 

tella 

nniḍen  ur  d-nban  ara  ur  llin  ara 
am wid twalaḍ seg teɣmert ideg 
telliḍ.  Imeɣnasen  n  tugdut  ula  d 
nutni  ṭṭuqten,  acukan  yal  yiwen 
yeṭṭef  axjiḍ-is,  bɣiɣ  ad  d-iniɣ 
yeṭṭef  imi-is,  taswaɛt  qqerriḥet, 
teẓmek,  wigi  sya,  wid-nniḍen 
sya,  sani  ara  terreḍ  aqerru-k  a 
win yettnadin abrid n tugdut.
Wehran, xas akken d yir tallit, ur 
tɛedda  ara  fell-as  ccedda  am 
temnaḍin  nniḍen  n  tmurt  deg 
tallit-nni, tella tudert dinna ;yella 
ccna,  amezgun  mazal-it  yedder, 
amennuɣ ɣef tugdut ibedd s wid 
yumnen  yis-s,  anda  i  ak-yehwa 
ddu,  tamacint  telḥa  kecc  fren 
anwa abagut ideg ara tedduḍ. Ula 
d amennuɣ ɣef yidles d tutlayt n 
tmaziɣt yella, yeqwa, ziɣ ṭṭuqten 
yimeɣnasen, yal wa ansi d-yerza, 
anda yeɣra, aḥlil ɣef win ur neẓri 
atmaten-is acu i ten-yerḥan?
Ass-nni qrib d 20 seg yebrir deg 
yiseggasen  n  90,  tasdawit  akk 
teččur  d  imeɣnasen,  wigi  akk  d 
inelmaden n tesdawit yal wa acu 
n ukabar iɣer yettekka, maca ass-
nni, err tacact-ik deg yidi-s, ass-a 
d ass n yidles, d ass n umennuɣ, d 
ass  n  tlelli,  d  ass  n  tmeslayt  n 
ugdud amenzu n wakal-agi.
Ass-nni  yif  akk  ussan,  ziɣ  deg 
waṭas yid-neɣ i nella, inelmaden 
heggan-d  timzikiiyin,  isaragen, 
segmi  yuli  wass  armi  d-yeɣli 
ṭṭlam  tamdint  akk  tessawal  s 
tmaziɣt,  ass-nni  awal  yettezzi-d 
ɣef Lmulud At Maɛmar, tigejdit 
n  umennuɣ  aggagan,  akked  wid 
yellan d imekraf deg tallit n tefsut 
n  tmanyin,  Wuhran  tezher  ama 
deg  tesdawit  ama  di  berra,  ula 
tidukkla 
deg  yiɣrem-a,

Mazal anfafad yettaẓ ɣer sdat di Lezzayer 
Akman.  Aqader  n  ukman  d  tɣimit  deg  yixxamen  akked  uḥezzeb 
akken iwata lḥal. Annect-a, ssawalen-d ar ɣur-s waṭas n yimejjayen 
d yimassanen n tujjya. D nutni i yeẓra addad n sbiṭarat n tmurt.

yigejdanen 
lemɛawna », i d-tessefhem Massa 
Georgieva,  ɛla  ḥsab  n  tnegga  n 
AFP  d-yessawḍen  isali.  Timura-
agi  zemrent  ad  sutrent  alma  d 
145% n wamur-nsent ɣur FMI.
Tuddsa  n  FMI  tɛeggen-d  ass  n 
tlata  belli  coronavirus  amaynut 
ad  d-teglu  aseggas-a  s  tezɣent 
tadawsant urǧin neḍri seg tezɣent 
tameqrant  n  yiseggasen  1930. 
PIB  amaḍlan  ad  yenɣes  s  3%, 
yezmer  ugar,  ma  yella  tazmiḍalt 

ur  teḥbis  ara  i  sya  ɣer  taggara 
n  yunyu  u  ma  yella  akman  ad 
ikemmel  deg  umesḍis  wis  sin  n 
useggas-a.

teglizit « Great Lockdown ») ad

idularen  i  tdamsa  tamaḍlant  di 
2020  d  2021,  meḥsub  «  ugar 
tdawsiwin  n  Japon  akked 
n 
Lalman 
d-yessefhem 
i

Gita Gopinath.

Akman. Aṭas n waɣiren n tmurt

yeɛni s teɣzi n mraw n waussan.
mass 
Aneɣlaf 
Abdelaziz  Djerad 
iberreḥ-d  s 
uselḥem n ukman s teɣzi n mraw 
n  wussan.  Ad  ikemmel  ukman 
akken yella alamma d ass 29 deg 
mayyu  i  d-iteddun,  syin  ad  iban 
ma yella ad ikemmel ukman neɣ 
ad  yettwakkes.  Yenna-d  daɣen 
ilugan n ukman ad yeqqim akken 
yella deg waṭas n waɣiren n tmurt 
yeɛni seg 15h00 n tmeddit alamma 
d  07h00  n  tsebḥit  yettwagdel 
uḥerrek  ɣef  yimdanen  anagar 
wid  yesɛan  tesriḥ.  Ma  yella  d 
aɣir  n  Blida  akman  ad  yeqqim 
akken  d  ummid, 
tettwamnaɛ 
tuffɣa  n  medden  seg  waɣir. 
Awexxer-a  deg  ukman  swacu  i 
d-iberreḥ  uneɣlaf  amezwaru  ur 
d-yelli  ara  kan  akka  yella-d  ɣef 
snat  n  tmental.  Tamezwarut  d 
aḥezzeb  mgal  anfafad  Corona,  i 
mazal yeẓẓa tuccar-is deg tmurt, 
imi  llant  ar  tura  2534  n  lḥalat, 

yella-d  fell-asent  uwekked  sɣur 
usudu Pasteur. Ma yella d lmutat 
llant  367.  Yal  tikkelt  ttilint-d 
lḥalat  timaynutin.  Tis  snat  d 
addam  n  uselway  n  tegduda 
mass  Abdelmadjid  Tebboune  s 
yiwellihen n Tuddsa Tamaḍlant n 
Tdawsa i d-yeffɣen tikkelt yezrin 
ɛinani  mgal  timura  i  yekksen 
akman uqbel lawan. 
Seg  wayen  i  d-iberreḥ  uneɣlan 
amezwaru n tmurt, aɣir n Blida ad 
teqqim  deg  ukman  ummid.  Llan 
daɣen tẓa n waɣiren yettuḥettem 
ɣef  yimezdaɣ  ad  kemnen  seg  
15h00 n tmeddit alamma d 07h00 
n  tsebḥit,  lwilayat  yettwaɛnan  s 
ukman-a  d  ti  :  Béjaïa,  Tlemcen, 
Tizi Ouzou, Alger, Sétif, Médéa, 
Oran,  Tipaza  et  Aïn  Defla.  Deg 
taggara  yenna-d  38  n  waɣiren-
nniḍen  ad  kemnen  seg  19h00  n 
tmeddit alamma 07h00 n tsebḥit.
Mačči  d  tikkelt  tamezwarut  ara 
yettwawexxer ukman, ta d tikkelt 
tis  snat.  Tikkelt 
tamzewarut 
tella-d  alamma  d  19  deg  yebrir 
n  useggas  deg  wacu  nella.  Tura 
atan  yettwaselḥem  alamma  d 
29  deg  mayyu  n  useggas-a.  Ad 
yettwakkes  ukman-a  deg  wacu 
nella  mi  ara  yettwaqṭaɛ  unfafad 
Corona seg tmurt-nneɣ.

Tiɣremt  -  Un 42   Arim 20 yebrir 2020

Akemmel n umahil n urmud adamsan
Tannaḍin timaynutin n Djerad i 
yineɣlafen d yiwaliten
Amahil.  Djerad  yesmekta-d  belli  «irmad  yettwaɛnan  s  tannaḍin 
d  irmad  yettqabalen  imezdaɣ  s  waṭas  akked  yirmad  yezmer  ad 
sneṭḍen avirus-agi, ma d irmad nniḍen ur ten-teɛni ara temsalt, ilaq 
ad kemmlen deg uxeddim-nsen».

i 

yineɣlafen 

Abdelaziz 
yesuffeɣ-d 

Aneɣlaf 

amezwaru 
Djerad 
tannaḍin 
timaynutin 
d 
yiwaliten i usezgi d tuṭṭfa n urmud 
adamsan n tmurt d ureqqeɛ n kra 
temsal ur nteddu ara akken iwata 
di  tallit  tamezwarut  n  ukman 
yettuḥettmen  u  ara  yekfun  ass  n 
19 yebrir.
« Ar taggara n tallit tamezwarut n 
ukman, asiked n liḥala tadamsant 
teskanay-d  kra  n  yiɛewwiqen 
d-ttmagaren  ttawilat  n  ufares, 
tikwal  s  ufham  ur  nṣeḥḥa  ara 
n 
i 
teɣtasin  yeddem  unabaḍ 
umennuɣ  mgal 
coronavirus 
(Covid-19) », i yesḥassef uneɣlaf 
amezwaru  deg  tannaḍt-ines  n 
wass n larebɛa 15 di yebrir.
Djerad yesmekta-d belli « irmad 
yettwaɛnan  s  tannaḍin  d  irmad 
yettqabalen 
imezdaɣ  s  waṭas 
akked yirmad yezmer ad sneṭḍen 
avirus-agi,  ma  d  irmad  nniḍen 
ur  ten-teɛni  ara  temsalt,  ilaq  ad 
kemmlen deg uxeddim-nsen ».
Diɣen  «  tannaḍt  n  usuffeɣ  ɣer 
yimuras n 50% n yixeddamen deg 
uḥric adamsan, ur yeɛni ara aḥbas 
n  urmud,  maca  yeɛna  aseḥbiber 
ɣef tdawsa n yixeddamen-nneɣ i 
ilaq aed ḍefren alugen n lemḥadra 
ilaqen deg tallitin am tigi ».
« Dɣa, i usishel n lecɣal, ttawilat 
n  usiweḍ  n  yixeddamen  sɛan 
tesriḥ  ad  lḥun  »,  i  d-yesmekta 
uneɣlaf  amezwaru  yesḥasfen 
ɣef  «  wuguren  d-ibanen  xas 
akken tannaḍin d-yeffɣen banent, 
ttwafehment akken ilaq ».
I  tifrat  n  wuguren-agi,  Djerad 
yesunneḍ  iɛeggalen  n  unabaḍ 
akked iwaliten ad gen :
Afin  de  palier  à  ces  carences, 
Djerad a instruit les membres du 

tesriḥat  n 

Ɣef  ayagi,  iwaliten  ilaq  ad  rren 
deg ddehn-nsen timsal-agi :
1. Akemmel  n  urmud  di  lmersat 
ilexsen  akked  lmersat  ikiwanen. 
tikli  n 
Ɣef  aya, 
yixeddamen  n  lmersat  ilaq  ad 
ttwafkent di lawan, nnig n wakud 
yettunefken i ukman.
irmad 
2.  Deg  ayen  yeɛnan 
idamsanen yeḥwaǧen asikel berra 
n lwilaya, iwaliten yewwi-d fell-
asen ad fken tesriḥat n usikel gar 
lwilayat.
3.  Tesriḥat  n  tikli  ɣef  sebba  n 
uxeddim 
ttwasutrent 
ilaq  ad 
di  dayrat  anda  tella  tkebbanit 
tadamsant  neɣ  tadeblant  uɣur 
ttikin imsutren.
4.  Irmad  n  ttawilat  n  usiweḍ  n 
selɛa ur tessefk ara tesriḥ.
5.  Mi  ara  ittuserreḥ  i  yiwet  n 
tḥanut  ad  teldi,  ilaq  ad  ldin  ula 
d  anda  d-iqeṭṭu  am  leqwaq  n 
lǧemla.
6. Asikel n yiɣermanen s tkeryas-
nsen,  berra  n  wakud  n  ukman, 
yeqqim  d  ilelli,  ur  yeḥwaǧ  ara 
tesriḥ.

Blida,  anekcum  d 
tuffɣa  si 
lwilaya ttwagedlen i yiɣermanen, 
ḥala wid umi iserreḥ lqanun.

tḥuna 
ittreqqiɛen  iselkimen  yeɛna  ula 
d  tiḥuna  yeznuzuyen  tilifun  neɣ 
ittefliksiyen.
8.  Akk  irmad  n  usiweḍ  n  selɛa 
sɛan tesriḥ n usikel berra n wakud 
n ukman.

n

amezwaru.

ɣer

1.  Iɛeggalen  n  unabaḍ  ilaq  fell-

Aneɣlaf n Yidles 
Tasɣunt tadelsant 
tamynut

Tasɣunt. Taneɣlaft n Yidles, 
Malika Bendouda tcar-d, ass n 
umhad (lexmis) deg Lezzayer 
tamaneɣt, taẓrigt n wuṭṭun 
amezwaru n tesɣunt tadelsant 
«Inziyaḥat» i icar uɣlif-is ddaw 
n usentel n «takti n ubeddel» 
la tt-ssedduyen «yimura akked 
waggagen izzayriyen».
Deg yiwen n ukatar, tebder-d 
tneɣlaft aheyyi n yiwet n tesgilt 
deg Ṛṛadyu ara msakin deg 
ṛṛadyu Idles ddaw n uzwel 
«Inziyaḥat FM» yal ass seg 
usrag wis 12H00 ɣer wis 17H00 
d tacrikt akked uɣlif n Teɣwalt.
Almend n Wass n Tmussni, 
tenna-d tneɣlaft dakken 
«imeẓla-s fkan azal ameqran 
i Wass-a, tesmekti-d dakken 
ineggura-a «la ttmahalen imira 
i wakken ad alsen asuddes n 
yimeẓla igensiyen n uɣlif i 
wakken ad yemmezgen akked 
yibeddilen yellan deg umaḍal».
Deg wayen yerzan wid ara yarun 
deg tesɣunt, tenna-d tneɣlaft 
dakken «tiwwura n uttekki 
deg tesɣunt-a ldint i wakk 
izzayriyen», tezzireg-d dakken 
afran n uzwel «Inziyaḥat» ila 
azal yerna akka i t-nebɣa.
Ɣef wakken i tettwali tneɣlaft, 
tasɣunt-a d akemmel, d asmal 
n ugbur akked uttekki deg tikci 
n uzal akked urafeq n yidles 
Azzayri.

Akli Smaɛni

21

Anfafad Covid-19
Lewṣaya i usuɣal 
n yiɣermanen 
izzayriyen yellan 
deg uzɣar

Lewṣaya. Iweṣṣa-d uneɣlaf 
amenzu, Abdelaziz Djerad, 
ineɣlafen ay terza temsalt 
akken ad d-ssuɣalen iɣermanen 
iweḥlen deg uzɣar deffir ma 
ssaglen, deg meɣres yezrin, 
amesni awlal d ugennan ɣef 
lǧal n tkaɣreft n unfafad 
bu uqacuc, ɣef wakken ay 
d-yenna, ass n usimwas, yiwen 
n ulɣu n yimeẓla n uneɣlaf 
amenzu. « S usnas n lewṣayat 
n Mass Aselway n Tegduda, 
iweṣṣa-d uneɣlaf amenzu, Mass 
Abdelaziz Djerad, aneɣlaf n 
yiweẓla iwerdaniyen, aneɣlaf 
n ugensu, tinbaziyin tidiganin 
d useqɛed n ugelluy d uneɣlaf 
n yimahilen inagduden d 
umesni akken ad d-bdun 
tamhelt n usuɣal n yiɣermanen 
yessakalen deg uzɣar yernu 
weḥlen din ɣef lǧal n usigel n 
umesni agennan d uwlal deg 
wayyur n Meɣres n 2020 ɣef 
lǧal n tkaɣreft n unfafad bu 
uqacuc n COVID-19 », ɣef 
wakken ay d-yenna ulɣu-a.
Ilmend n waya, yenna-d 
dakken iɣermanen ay terza 
temsalt yernu sɛan tinfulin 
n tuqqla ɣer Lezzayer 
ttwanecden-d akken ad 
ssiggzen, seg yimir-a, deg 
yisemlen-a n Internet: www.
pm.gov.dz – www.mae.gov.dz 
– www.interieur.gov.dz
Yessefk ad d-fken akk tilɣa ay 
yessefken akken ad ten-ḥesben 
yernu ad ten-nermsen.
Iɣermanen ara d-ssuɣalen ad 
ten-skemnen deg temṣukin ay 
d-yettwaheyyan i waya yernu 
ad ten-sfeqden yimsujjiyen, ɣef 
wakken ay d-yenna ulɣu-a.

Tanegga APS

Tiddukliwin tidelsanin n Tmurt n Leqbayel
Tiwizi i twaculin yenṭerren seg ukman

Tiwizi.  Akman  mgal  unfafad 
n  coronavirus,  yeǧǧa  aṭas  n 
twaculin tigellilin nṭerrent s waṭas 
deg  tɣiwant  n  Temrijet,  adabu 
ur  d-yeggir  ara  iman-is  ad  yili  i 
lmendad n yimeɣban imi akman 
yella war ma tella tezrawt s wayes 
zemren  yimezdaɣ  n  tama-a  ad 
bedden  mgal  lixṣaṣ  deg  yisufar 
n wučči, xirella ibabaten ur nesεi 
tijernaḍin  idumen,  d  ixeddamen 
n  wass,  ma  xedmen  ad  ččen  ma 
ur  xdimen  ara  ad  qqimen  i  llaẓ, 
ma teffɣeḍ ad temteḍ s unfafad n 
corona, ma teqqimeḍ ad temteḍ s 
llaẓ, tagnit d tin ikemren s waṭas, 
anect-a  yeǧǧa  kra  n  tddukliwin 
tidelsanin,  ad  ṭṭfent  taεkumt-a 
ẓẓayen mačči d kra. 
Azal  n  wayyur,  segmi  tefreq 
tddukla 
tanmettit 
tadelsant 
“TIWIZI” tamuddi n 90 iḍellaεen 
n  yisufar  n  wučči  ɣef  twaculin 
yenḥafen, yiwen seg yiɛeggalen-
is 
iwumi  qqaren  Fawzi  Ḥ 
yenna-d : « Ilaq ad nexdem ayen 

iwumi  nezmer  s  wayes  nezmer, 
ad nessiweḍ tagella i twaculin-a 
ma yebɣa Rebbi ad nessiweḍ azal 
n  200  iḍellaεen  uqbel  remṭan  i 
d-itteddun ». 
Itri azeggaɣ azzayri iqeddcen deg 
tɣiwant-a,  ula  d  netta  yexdem 
ddeqs  n 
tigawin  deg  wayen 
yerzan  tezdeg,  meḥsub  yal  ass 
itteffeɣ  s  yilmeẓyen  iqeddcen 
deg-s ad zzin i yiberdan n tɣiwant 
s ttawilat usizdeg, teddun axxam 
axxam,  abrid  abrid,  ula  d  nutni 
aṭas n yisufar n wučči d tedrimt, 
d  isufar  nessexdam  deg  tezdeg  i 
d-jemεen sɣur wid yegren Rebbi 
deg wulawen-nsen. 
Taddukla  Tadelsant  “ASURIF”, 
ula  d  nettat  tqeddec  i  wayen 
tezmer  iwakken  ad  d-tefk  afus 
n  lemεawna  i  wid  yestahlen, 
s  ujmaε  n  yisufar  n  wučči, 
xedmen  daɣen  yiwet  n  tigawt 
yelhan,  wwin-d  akettan  ferqen-t 
ɣef  lxalat  d  teqcicin  yessnen  ad 
tikmamin  ara 
xiḍent  ggant-d 

ferqen  ɣef  sbiṭarat  d  yemdanen 
ihelken  aṭṭan  ur  nḥellu  ara  d 
twaculin iḥaz waṭṭan n Covid-19. 
Tiddukliwin-a  daɣen  xemment 
amek i d-yewwi lḥal ad sdakklent 
tigawin-nsent  akken  ad  awint 
lfayda ugar, yerna ad ḥazen amur 
ameqqran  n  twaculin  yuḥwağen 
afud n lemεiwna.
Anect-a  yelha,  d  acu  mačči  d 
ayen ara d-yawin tifrat i yiɣeblan 
ttidiren  yemdanen  deg  tallit-a  n 
lḥers ssebba n uknam, ilaq ad tili 
tsertit  yemmuzgen  s  wayes  ara 
nerr aktar.
Deg  wussan-a  yezrin  aselway  n 
tigduda,  Ԑebd  Lmağid  Tebbun 
;  Yeṭṭef  yiwen  n  rray  d  akken 
ddula  ad  d-tefk  azal  n  umelyun 
n  ssunṭim  i  twaculin  yuḥwağen 
uqbel ayyur n remṭan i d-iteddun, 
rray  am  wa  yelha,  d  acu  ur 
yezmir  ara  ad  yefru  iɣeblan  n 
kra n yimeɣban, acu ara yexdem 
yiwen s wulac !

Aciri n yiwen n ukala n usetrer 
n yisuda unadi akerrazan

yikataren

Aciri.  Anadi.  Yella-d  uciri  n 
yiwen  ukala  n  usetrer  akked

Awal n uneɣlaf n waddal n tmurt n Ṭṭelyan ɣef telɣuɣa
Talɣuɣa.  Ugar  n  sin  n  yimalas 
segmi teḥbes telɣuɣa n ddabex n 
uḍar kalčyu n tmurt n Ṭṭelyan, d 
temsizlin n waddalen yemgaraden 
sebba  d  anfafad  n  corona  i 
d-yeglan s tmettant n ugar n tẓa n 
wagimen n yiṭṭelyanen.
Anfafad-a  i  d-ibanen  i  tikkelt 
tamezwarut  deg  tmurt  n  Ccinwa 
deg  wayyur  n  yennayer  yezrin 
icekkel  tuget  n  tmura  n  umaḍal, 
ibelleɛ  tikebbaniyin  timeqqranin 
akken  ur  belɛent  ara  yakan  ula 
deg tegnatin n ṭrad. Xlan yinurar 
d  yidgan  n  uḥewwes, 
tcuḥ 
tedrimt yezzi-d ureqqas n tdamsa 
tagreɣlant ɣer uḥric n tezmert.
Imdanen kemnen deg yixxamen-
nsen,  d  ta  kan  i  d  tifrat  i  d-ufan 
yimejjayen  d  yimnadiyen  ɣas 
akken  ɛerḍen  kra  n  ddwawi  i 
yellan  yakan,  Maca  ar  ass-a  ur 
d-tban ara ddwa yesseḥluyen seg 
waṭṭan-a s wudem unṣib.
Aneɣlaf  n  waddal  n  tmurt  n 
Ṭṭelyan  Finčunẓu  Sbadafura  d 
win  yekcem  ccek  ɣef  wazemz 
n  ukemmel  n  telɣuɣa  n  Kalčyu, 
akken i d-yenna qrib d awezɣi ad 
yili ukemmel-is sya ar wayyur n 
mayyu i d-iteddun.
Deg  umeslay  i  d-yefka  i  tliẓri 
“Ray  3”  n  tmurt  n  Ṭṭelyan, 
tazwara 
yesteɛref-d  akken  di 
ur  yenwi  ara  ad  yeddu  unfafad 
akka, ad iḥaz tamurt n Ṭṭelyan s 
tuget-a, d aymi i yenwa ad tuɣal 

telɣuɣa  deg  wussan  imenza  n 
wayyur  n  mayyu,  maca  tagnit 
i  tettidir  tmurt  ass-a  d  tin  i 
yuḥwaǧen  ugar  n  wussan  n 
ukman.Akken  i  d-yenna:  “Ɣas 
akken ad tuɣal telɣuɣa, timliliyin 
ad  ilint  war  imferǧen,  nessarem 
ad  yili  ukemmel-is  deg  tazwara 
n wayyur n mayyu maca ur ḥsiɣ 
imi ula d imejjayen d yimnadiyen 
ur  as-d-ufan  ara  tifrat  i  uɣbel-a 
iceklen amaḍal”.  
Finčunẓu  yeqqen 
azemz  n 
ukemmel  ɣer  tegnit  d  wayen  i 
d-nnan yimusnawen. Ɛlaḥsab-is d 
tazmert i yezwaren, ayen tettidir 
tmurt  n  Ṭṭelyan  ussan-a  werǧin 

tedder-itt  yakan  deg  akk  ceddat 
tesɛedda,  ass-a  tamurt-a  tuḥwaǧ 
taddukli  n  tarwa-s  iwakken  ad 
teffeɣ seg yir tagnit-a.
Akken  i  d-yerna:  “Mi  ara  tfak 
teswiɛt-a i aɣ-iceblen ad uɣalent 
temsal  akken  llant,  imir  rray  ad 
yuɣal i tdukkla taṭelyant n ddabex 
n uḍar, ad kemlent temliliyin deg 
unebdu  neɣ  ad  nadin  tifrat  acku 
timsal d tid iceklen s tidet”. 
Aneɣlaf n waddal n tmurt-a d win 
i  yuysen  ad  uɣalent  temliliyin 
akk  n  waddal,  Seld  ma  kfun 
wussan-a  iberkanen  d  addal  kan 
ara  d-yerren  tudert  ɣer  waɣiren 
yemgaraden n tmurt-nneɣ.

S. H.

Taɣamsa. Amer mazal adabu yettuqecɛen s ugdud d-iteffɣen nnig useggas 
ar ubrid, Bouteflika d wid-is, ad yegzu timsal yiwen imi werjin ad yili uɣmis 
La Cité ddaw tqeccabit-is. Deg tallit-a n Ammar Belhmir di tesga n taywalt, 
wissen anwa yellan deffir n uḥbas ?
