Anwa i d Amaziɣ assa !?
Tamaziɣt  d  tamagit 
n  yiɣerfan  n  tferka 
ugafa.  D  tutlayt  n 
tmurt  n  Tmazɣa.  D 
isirew  n  tutlayin  d 
tantaliwin  i  d-yefru-
rin  seg-s.  Tamaziɣt 
d  askar  n  tudert,  d 
iziɣer  n  yiɣerfan 
tesduri.  Anwa  i  d 
Amaziɣ ass-a ? Amek-it umaziɣ ass-a 
? Ihi ! Amaziɣ mačči d asfugel-nni kan 
n  tmeɣra  n  yennayer  d  n  20  yebrir. 
Mačči d ameɣnes deg uxxam deffir n 
uselkim. Amaziɣ d win yerran tamsalt 
n tmaziɣt d tin umenzay, d tin n yiseɣ 
d  nnif  d  lḥerma. Amaziɣ  ass-a  d  win 
yesnen  amezruy-is,  d  win  ur  nenkir 
ara laṣel-is, d win yerran amennuɣ ɣef 
tmaziɣt  d  tazwart  n  tzewwarin,  d  as-
dag n tmagit d tillit-is. Amaziɣ ass-a d 
win  yefkan  isem  amaziɣ  i  tarwa-s,  d 
win yerran azal i tudert n yimenza, d 
win yeṭṭfen deg wansayen, deg tgem-
mi d yiṣuḍaf tesduri tejmaɛt n taddart. 
Amaziɣ  ass-a  d  win  yettmeslayen  i 
dderya-s  s  tutlayt-nsen  tayemmat,  d 
wi yeẓẓan axalaf neɣ tileqqimt. Ama-
ziɣ ass-a d wi yessebɣasen kra yellan 
d  tisuffɣin  n  tsekla  d  ccna  d  yisura  s 
tutlayt  tamaziɣt. Amaziɣ  d  wi  yesɣan 
ungal n tmaziɣt d usebɣes n yimyura. 
Amaziɣ  ass-a  d  yal  Aqbayli,  Acawi, 
Amẓabi, Acenwi, Atergi, Acelḥi, Arifi, 
Akanari, am nutni am lxalat-nsen, am 
dderya-nsen ɛeqlen iman-nsen d acu-
ten. Amaziɣ ass-a d tamsetla d leqḍer 
gar  yimaziɣen,  d  usdakkel  n  umen-
nuɣ, d ufraz n tmuɣliwin tatrarin timay-
nutin i usbeddi n tmurt n Tmazɣa. Ad 
d-nefren ad nessikmel tamuɣli. Anida 
yella  kra  n  umaziɣ  iseḥḥan  ad  t-ne-
qsed ad t-nesseḥḍer. Yeqqeṛs ṭbel ye-
fra  wurar. Amennuɣ  yettkemmil.  I  te-
bɣuḍ  iɣzif  ay  iḍ,  d  uleqrar  ad  d-yali 
wass. 

K. S.

Ar  tura,  takenbanit  yessizrigen  Ayalas 
Tiɣremt akked La Cité, teṭṭef wissen ma 
tezmer ad ternu nnig waya ladɣa imi tt-
rran ar rrif ! D acu tugdi-s d tin yugaren 
aya,  xersum  di  tkebannit  ur  nesɛi  ara 
imɛelmen.  Imi  ineɣmassen  deg  sin  n 
yiɣmisen  win Tiɣremt  akked  win  n  La 
Cité,  mačči  d  menwala.  «  Ineɣmassen 
yellan di sin n iyalassen-a d wid yesɛan 
iseɣ d wawal imi d imeɣnassen n unnar, 
d  wid  yettgalan  s  ğmaɛliman  alama 
ikemmel  umecwar  ay  d-bdan  iwakken 
ad tidir tutlayt d win n uzref ɣer yisali, 
ladɣa  d  tarrayt  iwakken  ad  temhaz 
tmaziɣt  ad  tezger  i  ugemmaḍ  akin  »,  s 
wacu i yekfa awal-is Fodil Mezzali.

Beramtane Amimeur 

Tugna n wass-a

Ilmend n tefsut n Yimaziɣen d ukman i d-iḥettem unfafad n Corona, snulfan-d 
tikmamin s wannay amaziɣ. Amedya i d-yeskanayen amek i ṭṭfen Yimaziɣen deg 
tumast-nsen s zzux d usbeyyen-ines.

Aɣmis  iwmi  qqaren  La  Cité,  d 

ayalas  aɣelnaw  s 
tutlayt  n 
tefransist, d win i d-yufrarren ass 
n 20 yebrir 2013. Imi i d as-yettwakkes 
udellel sɣur l’ANEP, ur d-yeffiɣ ara ugar 
n wayyur ar tura. Ur yezmir ad yeqqim 
war  ma  yettekka  akked  yimaɣriyyen-is 
d wid n Tiɣremt, i d-yettefɣen s tutlay n 
tmaziɣt,  «  lferḥ  d  yiseɣ  s  win  ara 
yesfugel  amuli-s  wis  7  s  tmagit  i 
d-yebdan tettaɣ aẓar deg uẓar n tmurt », 
i  d-yenna  Fodil  Mezzali,  anemhal  n 
uɣmis  n  La  Cité.  Dɣa,  i  wid  d  tid  ur 
neẓri, d Fodil Mezzali d uɣmis-ines La 
Cité  i  d-yellan  deffir  n  tuffɣa  n  uɣmis 
awḥid i d-iteffɣen s tmaziɣt deg tmurt n 
Lezzayer, ahat deg Tferka n Ugafa.
«  Nmugger  s  lferḥ  awal  i  aɣ-d-yefka 
uneɣlaf  amaynut  n 
teywalt,  Mass 
Ammar Belhimer, imi yenna ad iwenneɛ 
aḥarar d leqdic s wudem yelhan xersum 
deg uḥric yerzan tid n udellel i yiɣmisen 
d-tettakk  tkebbanit  n  unabaḍ  ANEP  » 
akken i d-yerna yenna. Dɣa, ar taggara : 
« ar tura, azal n durt, ayalas la Cité d win 
yettidirren ussan n lḥers imi yettwakkes-
as waṭas n yizerfan-is, ur yesɛi sani ara 
s-d-tekcem 
imi  akka  ass-a 
yedder ala s snat n tefrawin n udellel », 
d-iwekked  unemhal  n  uɣmis.  Asḥisef 
imi, yeɛni agdud iwala-t yakkan anecta, 
imi  wid  yeddan  d  leḥkem,  asurḍi  d 
tzeɣwin i uɣmis-ines deg uxxam n Tahar 
Djaout. Dɣa, dg temslat-a, yenna Fodil 
Mezzali  :  «  tuget  seg  wid  yeddan  deg 
ubrid n lmunda wis-5. Ula yiwen uɣmis 
seg-sen  ma  yella-d  fell-as  ayen  yuɣen 
ayalas la Cité, xersum deg lmunda wis-4 
d uneggaru anida teɣli-d fell-as tezɣent 
n tedrimt. »
Wid  iḍefren  timsal  n  tɣamsa  d  teywalt 
deg  tmurt,  yeẓra  acḥal  n  yiɣmisen  i 
iḥebsen  ɣef  ssebba  n  lxilaf  akked  wid 
iḥekkmen tamurt. Necfa akk i tedyant n 
uyalas Le Matin i yesseḥbes uselway n 

tedrimt 

yettwakksen,  Abdelaziz 
Tegduda 
Bouteflika. Nnig waya, yerna yessekcem 
ar  lḥebs  anemhal-ines  Benchikou,  ɣef 
ssebba  ur  nelli.  Ma  telliḍ  anɛam  sidi, 
Teɛrefni  nɛerfek”,  kulci  yeslhel,  cuf 
aqendur i Sid-ik, ad terwuḍ lulu d cucu. 
Aɣmis  n  La  Cité,  imi  daɣen,  yellan 
deffir n usufeɣ n uyalas awḥid s tmaziɣt, 
ddan fell-as, kkren-as ad t-kksen.
Ayɣer adabu yebɣa ad yesseɣli ayalas la 
Cité imi i s-yeḥbes adellel ? Kra seg wid 
yessnen  annar  n  tɣamsa  la  d-qqaren  d 
akken ɛuqben-t imi la yefka azal i tutlayt 
n tmaziɣt. Seg wasmi d-yella uyalas La 
Cité, netta yessufeɣ deg tazwara rebɛa n 
yisebtar s tmaziɣt, yezger ar umayyur s 
tmaziɣt, almi d-yewweḍ ass-a yessueɣ-d 
s yidrimen-is aɣmis yellan gar yifassen-
nwen  Tiɣremt.  Aṭas  i  d-yeqqaren  d 
sebba taḥeqqanit d ta.
Ahat,  amer  mazal  adabu  yettuqecɛen  s 
ugdud d-iteffɣen nnig useggas ar ubrid, 
Bouteflika  d  wid-is,  ad  yegzu  timsal 
yiwen imi werjin ad yili uɣmis La Cité 
ddaw tqeccabit-is. Deg tallit-a n Ammar 
Belhmir di tesga n taywalt, wissen anwa 
yellan deffir n uḥbas ? « Ur ilaq ara ad 
nettu d aneɣlaf yellan ass-a ɣef uqerruy 
n Teywalt, Ammar Belhimer, i d-yefkan 
tesriḥ iwakken ad yili uɣmis s tutlayt n 
tmaziɣt.  Werjin  yefka-t-id  uneɣlaf  neɣ 
uselway deg umezruy n tefriqt ugafa. D 
acu d netta yellan-d ɣer yidis-is Usqamu 
Unnig  n  Timuzɣa,  HCA. Asmi  yemlal 
ugur n usufeɣ n uyalas Tiɣremt, ar tura d 
win  yettnaɣen  ɣer  yidisan  n  HCA 
iwakken ad yettwakkes lḥers i d-yellan 
ɣef  uyalas  Tiɣremt  s  tutlayt  n  tmaziɣt 
ladɣa  iwakken  ad  yuɣal  ɣer  wannar  n 
tɣamsa  taɣlnawt  »,  ilmend  i  wayen  i 
d-yenna  Fodil  Mezzali.  Ata  d  acu  i 
iḥeyren unemhal n La Cité yerna mazal 
yesteqsay  ayɣer  s  ulac  n  udellel  sɣur 
ANEP  imi  aṭas  n  twaculin  i  yeddren  s 
uɣmis.
